### [32] [Repeated Deceptive Path Planning against Learnable Observer](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07174v1)
*Shiyue Cao,Pei Xu,Likun Yang,Lei Cui,Shizhao Yu,Shiyu Zhang,Yongjian Ren,Xiaotang Chen,Kaiqi Huang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 重复欺骗路径规划，涉及元学习适应，可启发agent规划与隐私。

TL;DR: 提出重复欺骗性路径规划（RDPP）问题并设计DeMP框架，通过双层优化应对学习型观察者，在持续欺骗中显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有欺骗性路径规划（DPP）假设观察者为静态非学习型，但真实场景中对手可通过历史轨迹学习适应；因此需要研究可学习观察者下的重复欺骗路径规划问题。

Method: 提出DeMP框架，包含回合级适应（短期调整策略）和元级更新（利用跨回合反馈学习观察者模型更新规律），以缓解增量更新导致的适应滞后。

Result: 实验表明DeMP在RDPP任务中显著优于现有方法，同时路径成本竞争力相当。

Conclusion: 建模与可学习对手的重复交互对持续欺骗至关重要，为多智能体系统中的欺骗与隐私研究提供新思路。

中文摘要：我们研究了欺骗性路径规划（DPP）问题，其中智能体旨在向外部观察者隐藏其真实目的地。虽然现有工作假设静态、非学习的观察者，但现实中的对手——例如在关键货物运输或军事行动中——可以通过从历史轨迹中学习来适应。为了填补这一空白，我们引入了重复欺骗性路径规划（RDPP），这是一种明确建模可学习观察者的新形式。我们表明，现有的DPP方法在此设置下失效，因为它们无法适应不断演化的对抗性预测。虽然将观察者先前的预测纳入更新可以实现某种适应，但这种增量更新会导致累积滞后，从而降低欺骗效果。为此，我们提出了欺骗性元规划（DeMP），这是一个双层优化框架，结合了回合级适应（实现短期策略调整以对抗更新的观察者）和元级更新（利用跨回合反馈来捕捉观察者如何更新其模型，并在未来回合中加速适应）。通过这种方式，DeMP减轻了适应滞后的积累，从而能够对学习型观察者维持持续的欺骗。跨环境的实验表明，DeMP在RDPP中显著优于现有方法，同时保持具有竞争力的路径成本。我们的结果强调了模拟与可学习对手重复交互的重要性，为多智能体系统中的欺骗和隐私提供了新见解。

Original abstract: We study the problem of deceptive path planning (DPP), where an agent aims to conceal its true destination from external observers. While existing work assumes static, non-learning observers, real-world adversaries-such as in critical goods transportation or military operations-can adapt by learning from historical trajectories. To address this gap, we introduce Repeated Deceptive Path Planning (RDPP), a new formulation that explicitly models learnable observers. We show that existing DPP methods fail under this setting, as they cannot adapt to evolving adversarial predictions. While incorporating observer previous predictions into updates enables some adaptation, such incremental updates cause accumulative lag that degrades deception. To this end, we propose Deceptive Meta Planning (DeMP), a two-level optimization framework that combines episode-level adaptation, which enables short-term policy adjustment to counter updated observer, and meta-level updates, which leverage cross-episode feedback to capture how observers update their models and accelerate adaptation in future episodes. In this way, DeMP mitigates the accumulation of adaptation lag, enabling sustained deception against a learning observer. Experiments across environments demonstrate that DeMP significantly outperforms existing approaches in RDPP while maintaining competitive path cost. Our results highlight the importance of modeling repeated interactions with learnable adversaries, providing new insights into deception and privacy in multi-agent systems.

### [34] [HMACE: Heterogeneous Multi-Agent Collaborative Evolution for Combinatorial Optimization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07214v1)
*Yuping Yan,Jirui Han,Fei Ming,Yuanshuai Li,Yaochu Jin*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 异构多agent协作进化框架，可迁移至自动代码优化agent协作。

TL;DR: HMACE是一种异构多智能体协作进化框架，通过角色专门化的智能体循环和记忆引导搜索，在NP-hard组合优化问题上取得了比现有LLM方法更好的质量-效率权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM-based方法依赖刚性模板的单体工作流，限制了记忆引导探索并导致过早收敛到局部最优，因此需要设计自主协作架构来克服这些局限。

Method: HMACE将每次进化迭代分解为四个协调智能体的循环：提议者探索策略，生成者合成可执行启发式，评估者进行经验评估，反思者基于存档更新记忆；并结合行为感知检索、轻量级候选过滤和适应度驱动的存档更新。

Result: 在TSP、在线BPP、MKP和PFSP上，HMACE实现了质量-效率权衡的改进；在LLM驱动参考中，TSP和在线BPP平均差距分别低至0.464%和0.223%，且消耗token数远少于基线。

Conclusion: HMACE通过异构多智能体协作和记忆引导搜索，有效提升了自动启发式设计的性能，避免了冗余评估和过早收敛。

中文摘要：大型语言模型最近成为针对NP-hard组合优化问题自动设计启发式算法的一种有前途的范式。尽管取得了进展，现有的基于LLM的方法通常依赖于受刚性模板约束的单体工作流，从而限制了记忆引导的探索，并导致过早收敛到局部最优。为了设计一种自主协作架构，我们引入了HMACE，一种异构多智能体协作进化框架，将启发式搜索重新概念化为组织设计问题。HMACE将每次进化迭代分解为一个自主的、角色专门化的循环，包含四个协调的智能体：提议者负责策略探索，生成者负责可执行启发式综合，评估者负责经验评估，反思者负责基于存档的记忆更新。通过结合行为感知检索、轻量级候选过滤和适应度驱动的存档更新，HMACE引导搜索朝向多样且有前途的启发式行为，同时避免冗余评估。在代表性COP（包括TSP、在线BPP、MKP和PFSP）上的广泛评估表明，与最先进的单智能体和多智能体基线相比，HMACE实现了良好的质量-效率权衡。在匹配的LLM驱动参考比较中，HMACE在TSP和在线BPP上取得了最低的平均差距（分别为0.464%和0.223%），同时这两个任务仅需0.13M和0.42M个token，远少于比较的基线。

Original abstract: Large Language Models have recently emerged as a promising paradigm for automated heuristic design for NP-hard combinatorial optimization problems. Despite this progress, existing LLM-based methods typically rely on monolithic workflows constrained by rigid templates, thereby restricting memory-guided exploration and triggering premature convergence to local optima. To design an autonomous and collaborative architecture, we introduce HMACE, a Heterogeneous Multi-Agent Collaborative Evolution framework that reconceptualizes heuristic search as an organizational design problem. HMACE decomposes each evolutionary generation into an autonomous, role-specialized loop with four coordinated agents: a Proposer for strategy exploration, a Generator for executable heuristic synthesis, an Evaluator for empirical assessment, and a Reflector for archive-backed memory update. By coupling behavior-aware retrieval, lightweight candidate filtering, and fitness-grounded archive updates, HMACE guides the search toward diverse and promising heuristic behaviors while avoiding redundant evaluations. Extensive evaluations on representative COPs, including TSP, Online BPP, MKP, and PFSP, show that HMACE achieves a favorable quality-efficiency trade-off compared to state-of-the-art single-agent and multi-agent baselines. In the matched LLM-driven reference comparison, HMACE achieves the lowest average gaps on TSP and Online BPP (0.464\% and 0.223\%, respectively), while requiring only 0.13M and 0.42M tokens for the two tasks, substantially fewer than the compared baselines.

### [35] [MEMOREPAIR: Barrier-First Cascade Repair in Agentic Memory](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07242v1)
*Yang Zhao,Chengxiao Dai,Mengying Kou,Yue Xiu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出agent记忆级联修复机制，对agent记忆管理有重要启发。

TL;DR: 提出MemoRepair，一种针对智能体记忆中派生工件级联更新问题的修复契约，通过屏障优先机制确保后继状态有效，实验表明可消除无效记忆暴露并降低修复成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 智能体记忆中的派生工件在源工件变更后仍可见并引导行动，导致级联更新问题，现有系统缺乏有效的修复机制。

Method: 提出MemoRepair，采用屏障优先级联修复契约，通过撤回受影响后代、从保留支持和修复前驱构建后继、仅发布闭合前驱集的后继，将修复问题转化为最大权重前驱闭包，用s-t最小割求解。

Result: 在ToolBench和MemoryArena上，MemoRepair将无效记忆暴露从69.8-94.3%降至0%，相对于穷举修复恢复91.1-94.3%验证后继，修复算子成本降低至0.57-0.76。

Conclusion: MemoRepair能有效解决智能体记忆的级联更新问题，消除无效状态影响，并在修复成本与效果间取得良好平衡。

中文摘要：智能体记忆随着任务演变而成为持久的派生工件：摘要、缓存输出、嵌入、习得技能和可执行的工具程序。当源工件因工具或API迁移而删除、更正或失效时，从该源工件派生的后代工件可能仍然可见，并凭借过时的支持来引导未来的行动。我们将这种失败模式形式化为级联更新问题，其中修复的目标是记忆存储的可见派生状态。我们提出MemoRepair，一种针对智能体记忆的屏障优先级联修复契约。一次修复事件引发从无效后代状态到验证后继状态的受控转换：受影响的后代在修复前被撤回，后继状态由保留的支持和当前接口下分阶段修复的前驱构建，并且重新发布仅限于经验证的前驱闭包的后继。该契约引发了一个标量化的修复选择问题，用于固定修复成本权衡。我们证明所引发的发布问题可归约为最大权重前驱闭包，并可通过单个s-t最小割精确求解。在ToolBench和MemoryArena上的实验表明，在完全影响溯源的情况下，Memorepair将无级联修复系统下69.8-94.3%的无效记忆暴露降低到0%。与穷举修复所有相比，它恢复了91.1-94.3%的验证后继，同时将归一化修复算子成本从1.00降低到0.57-0.76。

Original abstract: Agentic memory evolves across tasks into durable derived artifacts: summaries, cached outputs, embeddings, learned skills, and executable tool procedures. When a source artifact is deleted, corrected, or invalidated by tool or API migration, descendants derived from that source can remain visible and steer future actions with stale support. We formalize this failure mode as the cascade update problem, where repair targets the visible derived state of the memory store. We present MemoRepair, a barrier-first cascade-repair contract for agentic memory. A repair event induces a controlled transition from invalidated descendant state to validated successor state: affected descendants are withdrawn before repair, successors are constructed from retained support and staged repaired predecessors under the current interface, and republication is restricted to validated predecessor-closed successors. This contract induces a scalarized repair-selection problem for a fixed repair-cost tradeoff. We show that the induced publication problem reduces to maximum-weight predecessor closure and can be solved exactly by a single s-t min-cut. Experiments on ToolBench and MemoryArena show that, with complete influence provenance, MemoRepair reduces invalidated-memory exposure from 69.8-94.3% under systems without cascade repair to 0%. Compared with exhaustive Repair all, it recovers 91.1-94.3% of validated successors while reducing normalized repair-operator cost from 1.00 to 0.57-0.76.

</details>


### [36] [EnvSimBench: A Benchmark for Evaluating and Improving LLM-Based Environment Simulation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07247v1)
*Yi Liu,TingFeng Hui,Wei Zhang,Li Sun,Ningxin Su,Jian Wang,Sen Su*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM环境模拟基准，直接支撑agent训练与评估

TL;DR: 发现LLM模拟环境存在状态变化悬崖问题，并提出EnvSimBench基准和约束驱动流程以提升模拟可靠性，降低成本和幻觉。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM模拟环境存在幻觉和状态漂移等问题，破坏奖励信号并增加成本，需要量化评估和优化方法。

Method: 定义EnvSim Ability，构建含400样本、167环境的基准EnvSimBench，设计约束驱动模拟流程。

Result: 所有LLM在状态不变时表现完美，但多状态更新时失败；新流程减少幻觉，提高产出6.8%，降低90%以上成本。

Conclusion: EnvSimBench提供了诊断和优化路径，为可靠的环境模拟和可扩展代理训练奠定基础。

中文摘要：可扩展的AI代理训练依赖于交互环境，这些环境能够忠实地模拟代理动作的后果。手工构建的环境成本高昂、扩展脆弱，且从根本上受限于多样性。一个有前景的方向是用LLM模拟的环境替代手工构建的环境。然而，这一范式依赖于一个未经检验的核心假设：LLM能够准确模拟环境反馈。在实践中，LLM模拟的环境存在幻觉、逻辑不一致和无声状态漂移故障，这些故障破坏了代理的奖励信号，并加剧了该范式本应消除的构建成本。为解决这一差距，我们提出EnvSimBench，包含四项贡献：1) 我们首次对环境模拟能力（EnvSim Ability）进行了正式定义和操作化，将其作为可量化的研究目标。2) 我们构建了EnvSimBench，一个严格的基准测试，涵盖167个不同环境中的400个样本，配备可验证标签和沿三个轴细粒度难度分层。3) 系统评估表明，所有最先进的语言模型都存在普遍的状态变化悬崖：当环境状态保持不变时，它们在任务上达到近乎完美的准确率，但当需要同时更新多个状态时却灾难性地失败。这一发现揭示了EnvSim Ability是一个关键但尚未充分解决的能力差距。4) 我们设计了一个约束驱动的模拟流程，大幅减少了幻觉，将环境合成产出率提高了6.8%，并将成本降低了90%以上。总体而言，EnvSimBench既是一个诊断框架，也是一个可靠的基于LLM的环境模拟的实际优化路径，为可扩展的代理训练奠定了基础。代码和数据可在https://github.com/cookieApril/EnvSimBench获取。

Original abstract: Scalable AI agents training relies on interactive environments that faithfully simulate the consequences of agent actions. Manually crafted environments are expensive to build, brittle to extend, and fundamentally limited in diversity. A promising direction is to replace manually crafted environments with LLM-simulated counterparts. However, this paradigm hinges on an unexamined core assumption: LLMs can accurately simulate environmental feedback. In practice, LLM-simulated environments suffer from hallucinations, logical inconsistencies, and silent state drift failures that corrupt agent reward signals and compound the construction costs that the paradigm was designed to eliminate. To address this gap, we propose EnvSimBench with four contributions: 1) We provide the first formal definition and operationalization of Environment Simulation Ability (EnvSim Ability) as a quantifiable research objective. 2) We construct EnvSimBench, a rigorous benchmark covering 400 samples across 167 diverse environments, equipped with verifiable labels and fine-grained difficulty stratification along three axes. 3) Systematic evaluations reveal that all state-of-the-art language models suffer from a universal state change cliff: they achieve near-perfect accuracy on tasks when the environment state remains invariant, yet fail catastrophically when multiple states need simultaneous updates. This finding exposes EnvSim Ability as a critical yet largely unaddressed capability gap. 4) We design a constraint-driven simulation pipeline that substantially reduces hallucination, boosts environment synthesis yield by 6.8%, and cuts costs by over 90%. Overall, EnvSimBench serves as both a diagnostic framework and a practical optimization path for reliable LLM-based environment simulation, establishing a foundation for scalable agent training. Code and data are available at https://github.com/cookieApril/EnvSimBench

### [37] [Can Agents Price a Reaction? Evaluating LLMs on Chemical Cost Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07251v1)
*Yuyang Wu,Yue Huang,Shuaike Shen,Xujian Wang,Shuhao Zhang,Qiyao Xue,Weichen Liu,Runtian Gao,Jian Ma,Xiangliang Zhang,Olexandr Isayev*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 科学工具使用agent评估基准，可迁移至coding agent

TL;DR: 本文提出ChemCost基准，评估LLM在化学采购成本估算中的工具使用能力，发现最强模型仅达50.6%准确率，且受噪声影响严重，失败模式包括解析、集成、选择和工具使用等问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前科学工具使用的评估缺乏客观真实值，尤其是化学领域，现有方法依赖主观判断，无法进行精确量化评估。

Method: 构建包含1,427个反应的ChemCost基准，基于真实定价快照（2,261种化学品、230,775条报价），支持阶段级诊断；并设计噪声注入（别名、表达式、缺失字段、格式变化）测试鲁棒性。

Result: 最佳LLM智能体在干净输入上准确率仅50.6%（25%相对误差内），噪声注入后性能大幅下降；阶段分析显示失败主因包括解析脆弱、证据整合无效、包装选择错误及工具使用不收敛。

Conclusion: 工具访问对解决该任务必要但不充分，当前LLM在科学工具使用中仍存在显著缺陷；ChemCost为客观评估提供了有效基准。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）作为使用工具的智能体已变得越来越强大，其基准测试涵盖各种通用智能体任务。然而，对科学工具使用的严格评估仍然有限。在化学领域，最近的智能体能够规划合成并调用领域特定工具，但评估通常依赖于精心策划的演示、专家评估或基于LLM的评分，而不是精确且无需评判者的真实情况。我们通过化学采购成本估算来填补这一空白，这是一个实际任务，智能体必须确定化学物质身份、检索供应商报价、选择可购买的有效包装、归一化数量，并根据反应描述计算成本。我们引入了ChemCost，一个由1,427个可评估反应组成的基准测试，这些反应基于一个冻结的价格快照，涵盖2,261种化学物质和230,775条供应商报价，支持标量评分和阶段级诊断（包括基础认知、检索、采购和算术失败）。为了评估鲁棒性，我们进一步构建了受控的噪声注入视图，干扰化学别名、数量表达式、缺失字段和输入格式。对前沿、开源权重和化学专业化的LLM智能体的实验表明，工具访问对于解决任务来说是必要但不充分的。最强的智能体在干净输入上仅达到50.6%的准确率（相对误差在25%以内），并且在实际噪声下显著下降。阶段级分析进一步表明，失败源于脆弱的解析、无效的证据集成、无效的包装选择以及不收敛的工具使用。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have become increasingly capable as tool-using agents, with benchmarks spanning diverse general agentic tasks. Yet rigorous evaluation of scientific tool use remains limited. In chemistry, recent agents can plan syntheses and invoke domain-specific tools, but evaluations often rely on curated demonstrations, expert assessment, or LLM-as-judge scoring rather than exact, judge-free ground truth. We address this gap with chemical procurement cost estimation, a practical task in which an agent must ground chemical identities, retrieve supplier quotes, select valid purchasable packs, normalize quantities, and compute cost from a reaction description. We introduce ChemCost, a benchmark of 1,427 evaluable reactions grounded to a frozen pricing snapshot covering 2,261 chemicals and 230,775 supplier quotes, supporting scalar scoring and stage-level diagnosis of grounding, retrieval, procurement, and arithmetic failures. To evaluate robustness, we further construct controlled noise-injected views that perturb chemical aliases, quantity expressions, missing fields, and input formatting. Experiments with frontier, open-weight, and chemistry-specialized LLM agents show that tool access is necessary but insufficient for solving the task. The strongest agents reach only 50.6% accuracy within 25% relative error on clean inputs and degrade substantially with realistic noise. Stage-level analysis further shows that failures arise from brittle parsing, ineffective evidence integration, invalid pack selection, and non-convergent tool use.

### [38] [Structured Role-Aware Policy Optimization for Multimodal Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07274v1)
*Bingqing Jiang,Difan Zou*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多模态推理RL优化，角色感知credit分配可迁移至agent训练

TL;DR: 提出SRPO方法，通过角色感知的令牌级信用分配改进多模态推理中的RLVR，无需外部模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 序列级奖励无法区分令牌功能角色，导致难以验证正确答案是否得到视觉证据支持。

Method: 将响应分解为感知和推理令牌，利用自蒸馏的在线策略对比分配角色特定信用，并通过共享轨迹基线统一信号，得到正向令牌权重。

Result: 在多个多模态推理基准上，SRPO改进了基于证据的推理效果。

Conclusion: 角色感知的令牌级信用分配对于实现可靠的多模态推理至关重要。

中文摘要：基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR），尤其是结合分组相对策略优化（GRPO），在提升大型视觉语言模型（LVLMs）的推理能力方面展现出巨大潜力。然而，在多模态推理中，最终答案奖励通常在序列级别分配，不区分不同令牌的功能角色，因此难以确定正确答案是否得到与任务相关的视觉证据的支持。在本文中，我们从角色感知的令牌级别信用分配角度重新审视多模态RLVR，其中结构化响应被分解为用于提取视觉证据的感知令牌和用于从该证据推导答案的推理令牌。基于这一视角，我们提出结构化角色感知策略优化（SRPO），该方法在不改变奖励函数的情况下，将序列级GRPO优势细化为角色感知的令牌级优势。具体地，SRPO通过使用自蒸馏的在线策略对比来分配角色特定的信用：感知令牌根据其在原始与损坏视觉输入下的视觉依赖性被强调，而推理令牌根据其与生成感知的一致性被强调。这些角色特定信号通过共享的轨迹级基线进一步统一，产生正向令牌权重，调整相对更新幅度，同时保留原始GRPO奖励和优化方向，无需外部奖励模型或单独的教师。跨多个多模态推理基准的实验表明，SRPO改进了基于证据的推理，突出了超越均匀序列级信用向角色感知优化发展对于可靠多模态推理的重要性。

Original abstract: Reinforcement learning from verifiable rewards (RLVR), especially with Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), has shown strong potential for improving the reasoning capabilities of large vision-language models (LVLMs). However, in multimodal reasoning, final-answer rewards are typically assigned at the sequence level and do not distinguish the functional roles of different tokens, making it difficult to determine whether a correct answer is supported by task-relevant visual evidence. In this paper, we revisit multimodal RLVR from the perspective of role-aware token-level credit assignment, where structured responses are decomposed into perception tokens for extracting visual evidence and reasoning tokens for deriving answers from that evidence. Based on this perspective, we propose Structured Role-aware Policy Optimization (SRPO), which refines the sequence-level GRPO advantage into role-aware token-level advantages without changing the reward function. Specifically, SRPO assigns role-specific credit by using self-distilled on-policy contrasts: perception tokens are emphasized according to their visual dependency under original versus corrupted visual inputs, while reasoning tokens are emphasized according to their consistency with the generated perception. These role-specific signals are further unified through a shared trajectory-level baseline, yielding positive token weights that adjust relative update magnitudes while preserving the original GRPO reward and optimization direction, without requiring external reward models or separate teachers. Experiments across diverse multimodal reasoning benchmarks show that SRPO improves evidence-grounded reasoning, highlighting the importance of moving beyond uniform sequence-level credit toward role-aware optimization for reliable multimodal reasoning.

</details>


### [39] [Signal Reshaping for GRPO in Weak-Feedback Agentic Code Repair](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07276v1)
*Jia Li,Yuxin Su,Ting Peng,Hailiang Huang,Yuetang Deng,Michael R. Lyu*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 直接针对代码agent修复的RL信号重塑方法

TL;DR: 针对代码智能体强化学习中弱反馈问题，通过重塑GRPO的三种信号（结果语义、过程信用、组内可比性），显著提升编译与语义准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准GRPO在使用弱反馈（如仅编译成功信号）时，组内比较可能无效，因为信号缺乏语义排名、过程信用定位和组内执行可比性，导致策略优化偏差。

Method: 提出最小信号重塑构造：1）编译与语义分层奖励重塑轨迹排名；2）步骤级过程分数（超出组奖励归一化）重塑轨迹内更新强度；3）失败原因感知的回滚治理重塑组内可比性。保留GRPO的组归一化优势计算不变。

Result: 完整信号重塑GRPO将严格编译与语义准确率从0.385提升至0.535；分层奖励基础上加入过程分数加权使准确率从0.48升至0.53，平均评估步骤从23.50降至17.02。

Conclusion: 信号重塑有效解决了弱反馈下GRPO的局限，结果语义、过程信用与组内可比性三者缺一不可；特权词元级蒸馏等方法因信号稀释无法替代该框架。

中文摘要：代码智能体强化学习通常接收弱反馈：回滚时的信号是可靠且可执行的，但仅捕获任务成功的必要或表面条件，而非目标语义谓词。以智能体编译修复为设置，我们研究在此类反馈下标准GRPO的信号重塑。我们的核心主张是，GRPO的组内比较仅在三种信号被重塑后才有意义：结果奖励恢复语义排名，过程信号定位轨迹内信用，以及来自同一提示的回滚保持执行可比较。我们通过最小化信号重塑构造来操作化这些条件，该构造不改变GRPO的组归一化优势构造：编译与语义分层奖励重塑轨迹排名，组奖励归一化外的步骤级过程分数重塑轨迹内更新强度，以及失败原因感知的回滚治理重塑组内可比性。实验显示清晰的端到端增益：完整信号重塑的GRPO将严格编译与语义准确率从基础模型的零样本0.385提升至0.535。控制比较进一步解释了增益来源：二元奖励移除了仅编译的中间层并降低了轨迹控制；在分层奖励之上，过程分数加权将准确率从0.48提升至0.53，并将平均评估步骤从23.50减少至17.02。作为边界比较，特权提示词元级蒸馏主要优化局部分布对齐；在长工具使用轨迹中，该信号被非关键词元稀释，无法替代结果语义、过程信用或组内可比性。

Original abstract: Code-agent RL often receives weak feedback: rollout-time signals are reliable and executable, but capture only necessary or surface conditions for task success rather than the target semantic predicate. Using agentic compile-fix as the setting, we study signal reshaping for standard GRPO under such feedback. Our central claim is that GRPO's within-group comparison is meaningful only after three kinds of signals are reshaped: outcome rewards recover semantic ranking, process signals localize intra-trajectory credit, and rollouts from the same prompt remain execution-comparable. We operationalize these conditions with a minimal signal-reshaping construction that leaves GRPO's group-normalized advantage construction unchanged: compile-and-semantic layered rewards reshape trajectory ranking, step-level process scores outside group reward normalization reshape within-trajectory update strength, and failure-cause-aware rollout governance reshapes within-group comparability. Experiments show a clear end-to-end gain: full signal-reshaped GRPO improves strict compile-and-semantic accuracy from the base model's zero-shot $0.385$ to $0.535$. Controlled comparisons further explain the source of this gain: binary rewards remove the compile-only middle tier and degrade trajectory control; on top of layered rewards, process-score weighting further improves accuracy from $0.48$ to $0.53$ and reduces average evaluation steps from $23.50$ to $17.02$. As a boundary comparison, privileged-prompt token-level distillation mainly optimizes local distributional alignment; in long tool-use trajectories, this signal is diluted by non-critical tokens and cannot replace outcome semantics, process credit, or within-group comparability.

</details>


### [40] [SOM: Structured Opponent Modeling for LLM-based Agents via Structural Causal Model](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07301v1)
*Shiyue Cao,Pei Xu,Likun Yang,Lei Cui,Xiaotang Chen,Kaiqi Huang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 结构化对手建模框架，提升多agent策略推理

TL;DR: SOM通过两阶段框架（SCM构建+结构化推理）解耦对手建模与预测，在多个多智能体基准中显著提升LLM对手预测的准确性和稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法将对手建模与预测纠缠，依赖隐式推理，难以适应动态交互，故需解耦并显式建模因果结构。

Method: 提出结构化对手建模（SOM），分为两阶段：构建阶段使用结构因果模型（SCM）显式表示对手观察与动作的因果依赖；预测阶段LLM沿SCM路径进行结构化推理。

Result: 在多个多智能体基准测试中，SOM一致优于最先进的LLM推理基线，实现了更准确和可适应的战略决策。

Conclusion: SOM通过显式因果建模和结构化推理有效提升了对手预测能力，为复杂多智能体交互中的LLM智能体提供更强适应性。

中文摘要：准确预测对手行为是从交互中学习的大语言模型（LLM）智能体在多智能体和博弈论环境中的基本能力。现有方法通常将对手建模与预测纠缠在一起，依赖于隐式的上下文推理，限制了在动态交互中的适应性。为此，我们提出结构化对手建模（SOM），一个两阶段的对手建模框架，明确分离对手模型构建和对手预测。在构建阶段，SOM采用结构因果模型（SCM），这是一种基于图的变量依赖关系表示形式，来捕捉对手观察和行动之间的有向链接，产生显式且结构化的对手表示。在预测阶段，LLM沿着从SCM派生的清晰路径进行结构化推理，提高了预测准确性和稳定性。在多种多智能体基准测试上的广泛实验表明，SOM始终优于最先进的基于LLM的推理基线，在复杂和动态的多智能体交互中实现更准确和更具适应性的战略决策。

Original abstract: Accurately predicting opponents' behavior from interactions is a fundamental capability for large language model (LLM)-based agents in multi-agent and game-theoretic environments. Existing approaches often entangle opponent modeling with prediction, relying on implicit contextual reasoning and limiting adaptability in dynamic interactions. To this end, we propose Structured Opponent Modeling (SOM), a two-stage opponent modeling framework that distinctly separates opponent model construction and opponent prediction. At the construction stage, SOM employs a Structural Causal Model (SCM), a graph-based formalism for representing dependencies among variables, to capture directed links between opponents' observations and actions, yielding an explicit and structured opponent representation. At the prediction stage, the LLM performs structured reasoning along clear pathways derived from the SCM, improving both prediction accuracy and stability. Extensive experiments on diverse multi-agent benchmarks demonstrate that SOM consistently outperforms state-of-the-art LLM-based reasoning baselines, enabling more accurate and adaptable strategic decision-making in complex and dynamic multi-agent interactions.

### [41] [When Stored Evidence Stops Being Usable: Scale-Conditioned Evaluation of Agent Memory](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07313v1)
*Jiaqi Shao,Yiyi Lu,Yunzhen Zhang,Bing Luo*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出scale-conditioned agent记忆评估协议，属于通用agent评测方法。

TL;DR: 提出尺度条件评估协议，发现记忆体代理可靠性损失非单一，受代理、接口、规模和预算影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有记忆体评估仅报告固定快照准确率或检索质量，无法反映无关会话累积时证据的可维护性。

Method: 采用证据保持增长的尺度条件评估协议，固定任务证据并添加无关会话，记录代理-记忆轨迹，报告预算符合可靠性、尾部记忆调用负担、失败机制分解和可用规模边界四个诊断指标。

Result: 在LongMemEval上，HippoRAG保持两次调用预算内但预算符合可靠性下降16-20个百分点；LiCoMemory的失败依赖代理，Qwen3-8B超预算，Qwen3-32B和Qwen3-235B可靠。

Conclusion: 可伸缩记忆声明应基于代理、接口、规模范围和交互预算进行调整。

中文摘要：记忆体代理评估报告固定快照准确性或检索质量，但这些分数并未显示当无关会话（即未被注释为查询任务相关证据的会话）累积时证据是否仍然可用。我们提出了一种在证据保持增长条件下的代理记忆尺度条件评估协议：对于每个查询，任务证据保持不变，同时添加无关会话。该协议记录代理-记忆轨迹并报告四个诊断指标：预算符合可靠性、尾部记忆调用负担、失败机制分解以及可靠性低于目标的可伸缩性边界。将该协议应用于LongMemEval和LoCoMo，跨越平坦、平面和层次记忆接口，结果表明可靠性损失并非单一现象。在LongMemEval上，HippoRAG保持在两次调用预算内，但随着无关会话的添加，其预算符合可靠性下降了16-20个百分点；LiCoMemory的观察到的失败强烈依赖于代理，Qwen3-8B超出预算，而Qwen3-32B和Qwen3-235B在测试范围内保持可靠。结果支持了一个框架，即可伸缩记忆声明取决于代理、接口、规模范围和交互预算。

Original abstract: Memory-agent evaluations report fixed-snapshot accuracy or retrieval quality, but these scores do not show whether evidence remains usable as irrelevant sessions (sessions not annotated as task-relevant evidence for the query) accumulate. We present a scale-conditioned evaluation protocol for agent memory under evidence-preserving growth: for each query, task evidence is held fixed while irrelevant sessions are added. The protocol logs agent--memory trajectories and reports four diagnostics: budget-compliant reliability, tail memory-call burden, failure-regime decomposition, and the usable-scale boundary where reliability falls below the target. Applied to LongMemEval and LoCoMo across flat, planar, and hierarchical memory interfaces, the protocol shows reliability loss is not a single phenomenon. On LongMemEval, HippoRAG stays within the two-call budget but loses 16--20 percentage points in budget-compliant reliability as irrelevant sessions are added; LiCoMemory's observed failures depend strongly on the agent, with Qwen3-8B exceeding the budget while Qwen3-32B and Qwen3-235B remain reliable in the tested range. The result supports a framework for making scalable-memory claims conditional on agent, interface, scale range, and interaction budget.

Original abstract: Discovering governing differential equations from observational data is a fundamental challenge in scientific machine learning. Existing symbolic regression approaches rely primarily on quantitative metrics; however, real-world differential equation modeling also requires incorporating domain knowledge to ensure physical plausibility. To address this gap, we propose DoLQ, a method for discovering ordinary differential equations with LLM-based qualitative and quantitative evaluation. DoLQ employs a multi-agent architecture: a Sampler Agent proposes dynamic system candidates, a Parameter Optimizer refines equations for accuracy, and a Scientist Agent leverages an LLM to conduct both qualitative and quantitative evaluations and synthesize their results to iteratively guide the search. Experiments on multi-dimensional ordinary differential equation benchmarks demonstrate that DoLQ achieves superior performance compared to existing methods, not only attaining higher success rates but also more accurately recovering the correct symbolic terms of ground truth equations. Our code is available at https://github.com/Bon99yun/DoLQ.

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 将工具链视为连续流，提出agent推理新范式，涉及规划与工具使用。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have demonstrated remarkable capabilities in orchestrating tools for reasoning tasks. However, existing methods rely on a step-wise paradigm that lacks a global perspective, which causes error accumulation over long horizons and restricts generalization to unseen tools. To overcome these limitations, we propose Tools as Continuous Flow for Evolving Agentic Reasoning (FlowAgent), which reconceptualizes tool chaining as continuous trajectory generation within a semantic space. To systematically evaluate this paradigm, we introduce the first plan-level closed-loop benchmark dedicated to plan-level agentic reasoning in dynamic real-world environments. Specifically, the proposed FlowAgent leverages conditional flow matching to generate continuous latent trajectories, providing a global planning perspective to ensure coherent and robust tool execution. Theoretically, we establish formal bounds on utility convergence and prove that our continuous formulation fundamentally guarantees robust generalization and error attenuation. Empirical evaluations show that FlowAgent achieves superior robustness and adaptability in long-horizon reasoning tasks.

### [44] [GraphReAct: Reasoning and Acting for Multi-step Graph Inference](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07357v2)
*Xingtong Yu,Zhongwei Kuai,Chang Zhou,Xuanting Xie,Renhe Jiang,Xikun Zhang,Hong Cheng,Xinming Zhang,Yuan Fang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 将ReAct框架扩展到图推理，涉及推理-行动循环与动态上下文扩展，通用agent方法。

TL;DR: 提出GraphReAct框架，将推理-行动范式扩展到图学习，通过拓扑检索、语义检索和上下文精炼行动实现逐步推理，实验表明优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有推理-行动框架主要用于LLMs，未充分扩展到图学习，而图数据具有结构性和多步推理需求。

Method: 设计基于图的行动空间，包括拓扑检索、语义检索和上下文精炼，交织推理与行动，实现上下文扩展与压缩。

Result: 在六个基准数据集上持续优于最先进方法。

Conclusion: 验证了推理-行动对图学习的有效性。

中文摘要：推理-行动框架通过将推理与行动交织在一起以实现动态信息获取，从而增强了大型语言模型（LLMs）。然而，将该范式扩展到图学习仍然未得到充分探索。图数据具有内在的结构性，信息分布在节点和边上，并通过拓扑和潜在表示进行编码。因此，在图上的有效推理不仅需要从图中检索有信息量的证据，还需要在多步推理过程中逐步精炼累积的上下文。在这项工作中，我们提出了GraphReAct，这是一个图推理-行动框架，能够对图结构数据进行逐步推理。具体来说，我们设计了一个基于图的行动空间，包含两种互补的检索行动：拓扑检索，捕获局部结构依赖；以及语义检索，访问表示空间中非局部但相关的证据。这些行动动态扩展推理上下文。为了进一步支持多步推理，我们引入了另一种行动，即上下文精炼，它将累积的信息蒸馏并重组为紧凑的表示。通过将推理与检索和精炼行动交织，我们的框架实现了从上下文扩展到压缩的渐进过渡。在六个基准数据集上的大量实验表明，GraphReAct持续优于最先进的方法，验证了推理-行动对图学习的有效性。

Original abstract: Reasoning-acting frameworks enhance large language models (LLMs) by interleaving reasoning with actions for dynamic information acquisition. However, extending this paradigm to graph learning remains underexplored. Graph data is inherently structured, with information distributed across nodes and edges and encoded through both topology and latent representations. As a result, effective reasoning over graphs requires not only retrieving informative evidence from the graph, but also progressively refining the accumulated context during multi-step inference. In this work, we propose GraphReAct, a graph reasoning-acting framework that enables step-by-step inference over graph-structured data. Specifically, we design a graph-based action space with two complementary retrieval actions: topological retrieval, which captures local structural dependencies, and semantic retrieval, which accesses non-local but relevant evidence in the representation space. These actions dynamically expand the reasoning context. To further support multi-step reasoning, we introduce another type of action, context refinement, which distills and reorganizes accumulated information into a compact representation. By interleaving reasoning with both retrieval and refinement actions, our framework enables a progressive transition from context expansion to compression. Extensive experiments on six benchmark datasets demonstrate that GraphReAct consistently outperforms state-of-the-art methods, validating the effectiveness of reasoning-acting for graph learning.

</details>

中文摘要：开发轻量级的、设备上的视觉语言GUI智能体对于高效的跨平台自动化交互至关重要。然而，当前的设备上智能体受到模型容量有限的制约，进一步性能提升仍然迫切。针对小规模模型的传统监督微调（SFT）常导致过拟合、灾难性遗忘和策略僵化，因此无法完全应对这些挑战。在这项工作中，我们提出了一种新颖的免SFT训练范式，显著提升了小规模模型的性能。我们首次通过引导式在线蒸馏（Guided On-policy Distillation）将广义知识蒸馏系统性地整合到GUI智能体领域。通过结合预言参考轨迹和动态检索机制，我们的方法减少了幻觉，并缓解了多解GUI任务中固有的认知失调。在此基础上，我们进一步引入了多解双级GRPO框架，该框架联合对齐宏观级子任务规划与微观级执行匹配，从而改进长程GUI智能体场景中的探索。此外，我们构建了一个自动化数据生成管道，以合成带有丰富多解标注的GUI任务轨迹。大量实验表明，我们的方法在轻量级模型中达到了最先进的性能，同时在所有基准测试中与显著更大规模的模型保持竞争力。消融研究进一步证明，结构化在线蒸馏和多解双级探索可以完全释放2B/3B规模智能体的能力，超越传统模仿学习的性能极限。

Original abstract: Developing lightweight, on-device vision-language GUI agents is essential for efficient cross-platform automated interaction. However, current on-device agents are constrained by limited model capacity, and further performance improvements remain urgently needed. Traditional Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) for small-scale models often leads to overfitting, catastrophic forgetting and policy rigidity, and thus fails to fully address these challenges. In this work, we propose a novel SFT-free training paradigm that significantly enhances the performance of small-scale models. We first present the initial systematic integration of generalized knowledge distillation into the GUI agent domain via Guided On-policy Distillation. By incorporating oracle reference trajectories together with a dynamic retrieval mechanism, our method reduces hallucinations and mitigates the cognitive misalignment inherent in multi-solution GUI tasks. Building on this foundation, we further introduce a Multi-solution Dual-level GRPO framework that jointly aligns macro-level subtask planning with micro-level execution matching, thereby improving exploration in long-horizon GUI agent scenarios. In addition, we construct an automated data generation pipeline to synthesize GUI task trajectories with rich multi-solution annotations. Extensive experiments show that our method achieves state-of-the-art performance among lightweight models while remaining competitive with substantially larger-scale models across all benchmarks. Ablation studies further demonstrate that structured on-policy distillation and multi-solution dual-level exploration can fully unlock the capabilities of 2B/3B scale agents, surpassing the performance limits of conventional imitation learning.

Original abstract: Partially Observable Markov Decision Processes (POMDPs) are systems in which one agent interacts with a stochastic environment, and receives only partial information about the current state. In a multi-environment POMDP (MEPOMDP), the initial state is unknown, and assumed to be adversarially chosen. In this work we focus on computing the optimal value and policy in MEPOMDPs with finite-horizon objectives. That problem is known to be PSPACE-complete in POMDPs. Our main results are as follows: (1) we establish that it is also PSPACE-complete in the more general setting of MEPOMDPs; (2) we present a practical algorithm and evaluate it on classical benchmarks, significantly outperforming the only previously known algorithm.

### [47] [Open-Ended Task Discovery via Bayesian Optimization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07572v1)
*Masaki Adachi,Yuta Suzuki,Juliusz Ziomek*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 科学工作流中任务本身（优化目标和评估方法）会随证据积累而变化，传统贝叶斯优化忽视此不确定性，导致效率降低。

Method: 提出GSR框架，从种子任务开始，以粗到细方式生成新任务，并用任务获取函数调度优化过程，实现开放式贝叶斯优化。

Result: 在新产品开发、化学合成放大、算法分析和专利再利用等任务中，GSR优于现有基于LLM的优化器，且渐近遗憾仅比单任务BO多对数级。

Conclusion: GSR有效处理任务不确定性，在多种科学工作流中表现优异，为贝叶斯优化提供了开放式的框架。

中文摘要：当将贝叶斯优化应用于科学工作流时，一个主要但经常被忽视的不确定性来源是任务本身——即优化什么以及如何评估——随着证据的积累，这可能会发生变化。我们引入了生成-选择-精炼（GSR），一种开放式贝叶斯优化框架，在任务生成和任务优化之间交替进行。从用户提供的种子任务开始，GSR以由粗到细的方式生成新任务，同时任务获取函数调度优化。渐近地，它将评估集中在最佳任务上，相对于单任务贝叶斯优化仅产生对数遗憾开销。我们将GSR应用于新产品开发、化学合成放大、算法分析和专利再利用，其性能优于现有的基于大型语言模型的优化器。

Original abstract: When applying Bayesian optimization (BO) to scientific workflow, a major yet often overlooked source of uncertainty is the task itself -- namely, what to optimize and how to evaluate it -- which can evolve as evidence accumulates. We introduce Generate-Select-Refine (GSR), a open-ended BO framework that alternates between task generation and task optimization. Starting from a user-provided seed task, GSR generates new tasks in a coarse-to-fine manner while a task-acquisition function schedules optimization. Asymptotically, it concentrates evaluations on the best task, incurring only logarithmic regret overhead relative to single-task BO. We apply GSR to new product development, chemical synthesis scaling, algorithm analysis, and patent repurposing, where it outperforms existing LLM-based optimizers.

</details>


### [48] [Parallel Lifted Planning via Semi-Naive Datalog Evaluation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07584v1)
*Dominik Drexler,Oliver Joergensen,Jendrik Seipp*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 研究并行提升规划，基于半朴素Datalog，对agent规划方法有启发。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 提升式规划因反复实例化而速度慢，先前研究表明Datalog可用于其核心组件，但缺乏并行化研究。本文旨在通过并行Datalog执行加速提升式规划。

Method: 开发了两层并行Datalog执行模型（规则级和实例化级），并针对规划任务采用基于团枚举的实例化器，支持半朴素评估。使用FF启发式的贪心最佳优先搜索进行实验。

中文摘要：提升式经典规划器直接操作于一阶规划任务，以避免计算密集的实例化步骤。然而，提升式规划通常较慢，因为规划器必须在搜索过程中反复实例化基础结构。提升式经典规划的许多核心组件，如后继生成、公理评估、任务实例化和删除松弛启发式，先前已通过Datalog评估的视角进行了研究。我们在此工作基础上进行扩展，开发并分析了一个具有两个层次并行性的执行模型：规则级并行性和实例化并行性。我们进一步将此求解器专门化用于规划特定的工作负载，采用基于团枚举的实例化器，并扩展以支持半朴素Datalog评估。我们使用带有FF启发式的贪心最佳优先搜索进行的实验评估表明，我们的实现在单核上已经比基线解决了更多任务，并且随着使用更多核心，差距进一步扩大。此外，在难以实例化的任务中（平均97.6%的总运行时间花费在Datalog执行上），所提出的执行模型平均并行分数达到92.4%，在实际8核上实现了高达6倍的加速。

Original abstract: Lifted classical planners operate directly on first-order planning tasks to avoid the computationally demanding grounding step. However, lifted planning is typically slower, as planners must repeatedly instantiate ground structures during search. Many core components of lifted classical planning, such as successor generation, axiom evaluation, task grounding, and delete-relaxed heuristics, have previously been studied through the lens of Datalog evaluation. We build upon this line of work and extend it by developing and analyzing an execution model with two levels of parallelism: rule-level parallelism and grounding parallelism. We further specialize this solver for planning-specific workloads with a grounder based on clique enumeration, which we extend to support semi-naive Datalog evaluation. Our experimental evaluation using greedy best-first search with the FF heuristic shows that our implementation already solves more tasks than the baselines on a single core, and the gap widens as additional cores are used. Moreover, on hard-to-ground tasks where on average 97.6% of the total runtime is spent in Datalog execution, the proposed execution model exhibits an average parallel fraction of 92.4%, while achieving up to a 6-fold speedup on 8 cores in practice.

### [49] [Learning to Communicate Locally for Large-Scale Multi-Agent Pathfinding](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07637v2)

TL;DR: 提出LC-MAPF，一种带可学习通信模块的MAPF求解器，通过相邻智能体多轮通信提升协作，优于现有方法且保持可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有学习型MAPF求解器缺乏有效通信导致协作不足，本文旨在通过可学习通信模块增强智能体间合作以提高求解性能。

Method: 基于Dec-POMDP框架，每个智能体利用局部观测和相邻智能体通信信息决策；LC-MAPF采用可学习的多轮通信机制在相邻智能体间高效共享特征，并使用预训练模型实现泛化。

Result: 实验在多种未见测试场景中显示，LC-MAPF在多个指标上优于现有的IL和RL方法，且通信机制不牺牲可扩展性。

中文摘要：多智能体路径规划（MAPF）是多机器人轨迹规划问题中广泛使用的抽象，其中多个同质智能体在共享环境中同时移动。尽管最优求解MAPF是NP难的，但可扩展且高效的求解器对于物流和搜索救援等现实应用至关重要。为此，研究社区提出了各种利用机器学习的分散式次优MAPF求解器。这些方法将MAPF（从单个智能体视角）建模为Dec-POMDP，其中每个时间步智能体必须基于局部观测决定行动，并通常通过强化学习或模仿学习来解决问题。我们遵循相同方法，但额外引入了一个可学习的通信模块，通过高效的特征共享来增强智能体之间的协作。我们提出了局部通信多智能体路径规划（LC-MAPF），一种可泛化的预训练模型，该模型在相邻智能体之间应用多轮通信以交换信息并改善其协调。我们的实验表明，所引入的方法在多种（未见过的）测试场景中的多样指标上优于现有的基于学习的MAPF求解器，包括IL和基于RL的方法。值得注意的是，所引入的通信机制并未损害LC-MAPF的可扩展性，而可扩展性通常是基于通信的MAPF求解器的常见瓶颈。

Original abstract: Multi-agent pathfinding (MAPF) is a widely used abstraction for multi-robot trajectory planning problems, where multiple homogeneous agents move simultaneously within a shared environment. Although solving MAPF optimally is NP-hard, scalable and efficient solvers are critical for real-world applications such as logistics and search-and-rescue. To this end, the research community has proposed various decentralized suboptimal MAPF solvers that leverage machine learning. Such methods frame MAPF (from a single agent perspective) as a Dec-POMDP where at each time step an agent has to decide an action based on the local observation and typically solve the problem via reinforcement learning or imitation learning. We follow the same approach but additionally introduce a learnable communication module tailored to enhance cooperation between agents via efficient feature sharing. We present the Local Communication for Multi-agent Pathfinding (LC-MAPF), a generalizable pre-trained model that applies multi-round communication between neighboring agents to exchange information and improve their coordination. Our experiments show that the introduced method outperforms the existing learning-based MAPF solvers, including IL and RL-based approaches, across diverse metrics in a diverse range of (unseen) test scenarios. Remarkably, the introduced communication mechanism does not compromise LC-MAPF's scalability, a common bottleneck for communication-based MAPF solvers.

### [50] [Finite-Time Analysis of MCTS in Continuous POMDP Planning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07703v1)
*Da Kong,Vadim Indelman*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 连续POMDP中MCTS有限时间分析，涉及规划理论，对agent规划有潜在启发。

TL;DR: 本文为POMDP中的MCTS提供了有限时间分析，通过多项式探索奖励和Voronoi分区方法给出浓度界，并提出Voro-POMCPOW算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MCTS在POMDP中取得经验成功，但由于非平稳性和启发式动作选择导致的相互依赖性，缺乏严格的有限时间保证。

Method: 针对离散观测空间，将多项式探索奖励扩展到POMDP的UCB中；针对连续观测空间，提出抽象分区框架，并设计Voro-POMCPOW算法，使用Voronoi单元自适应分区，保持有限分支因子。

Result: 在离散设置得到多项式浓度界，连续设置得到高概率界；实验表明Voro-POMCPOW在提供理论保证的同时性能有竞争力。

Conclusion: 本文填补了POMDP中MCTS有限时间分析的空白，技术可推广至连续MDP。

中文摘要：本文针对部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程（POMDP）中的蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS）提出了有限时间分析，在离散和连续观测空间下给出了概率浓度界。尽管像POMCP这样的MCTS风格求解器在许多应用中取得了经验上的成功，但由于启发式动作选择（如UCB）导致的非平稳性和相互依赖性，严格的有限时间保证仍然是一个开放问题。在离散设置中，我们通过将多项式探索奖励扩展到POMDP设置中的UCB来解决这些挑战，为根节点处的经验值估计提供了多项式浓度界。对于连续观测空间，我们引入了一个抽象分区框架，并提出了分区损失的有限时间界。在温和条件下，我们证明了具有连续观测空间的POMDP中值估计的高概率界。具体来说，我们提出了Voro-POMCPOW，它是POMCPOW的一个变体，具有有限时间保证，使用Voronoi单元自适应地划分连续观测空间。这种方法在保持原始观测生成器的同时维护了有限的分支因子。实验验证表明，所提出的Voro-POMCPOW在提供理论保证的同时表现出有竞争力的性能。尽管我们的分析集中在连续POMDP上，但本文开发的技术也适用于连续MDP，填补了MDP方面的另一个空白。

Original abstract: This paper presents a finite-time analysis for Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS) in Partially Observable Markov Decision Processes (POMDPs), with probabilistic concentration bounds in both discrete and continuous observation spaces. While MCTS-style solvers such as POMCP achieve empirical success in many applications, rigorous finite-time guarantees remain an open problem due to the nonstationarity and the interdependencies induced by heuristic action selection (e.g., UCB). In the discrete setting, we address these challenges by extending the polynomial exploration bonus to UCB in POMDP setting, yielding polynomial concentration bounds for the empirical value estimation at the root node. For continuous observation spaces, we introduce an abstract partitioning framework and propose a finite-time bound on partitioning loss. Under mild conditions, we prove highprobability bound on value estimates in POMDPs with continuous observation space. Specifically, we propose Voro-POMCPOW, a variant of POMCPOW with f inite-time guarantees that adaptively partitions the continuous observation space using Voronoi cells. This approach maintains a finite branching factor while preserving the original observation generator. Empirical validation demonstrates that the proposed Voro-POMCPOW shows competitive performance while providing theoretical guarantees. Although our analysis focuses on continuous POMDPs, the techniques developed herein are also applicable to continuous MDPs, closing another gap on the MDP side.

### [51] [Hierarchical Task Network Planning with LLM-Generated Heuristics](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07707v2)
*Felipe Meneguzzi,Alexandre Buchweitz,Augusto B. Corrêa,Victor Scherer Putrich,André Grahl Pereira*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 研究大型语言模型能否为HTN规划生成有效搜索启发式，实验表明LLM生成的启发式接近最佳HTN规划器性能，并减少了搜索努力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: HTN规划中的启发式方法信息量不足，不如经典规划中的启发式有效，因此探索使用LLM生成更优启发式。

中文摘要：HTN规划是经典规划的一种变体，它不是搜索一个线性的动作序列，而是使用方法库将高层任务分解，直到只剩下可执行的动作。一方面，这允许通过方法库引入领域知识，从而加速解决方案的搜索。另一方面，它带来了超越经典状态空间搜索的挑战。尽管最近的研究产生了一些加速HTN规划的启发式和新型算法，但这些启发式方法的信息量仍然不如经典规划算法中的启发式。我们研究大型语言模型（LLM）是否能够为HTN规划生成有效的搜索启发式，将Corrêa、Pereira和Seipp（2025）的方法从经典规划扩展到层次规划。使用Pytrich规划器在六个标准全序HTN基准领域上，我们评估了在领域特定提示下由九个LLM生成的启发式，并将其与TDG和LMCount领域无关基线以及PANDA规划器进行比较。我们的结果表明，LLM生成的启发式几乎达到了最佳可用HTN规划器的覆盖范围，同时在83%的共享问题上显著减少了搜索努力。

Original abstract: HTN planning is a variation of classical planning where, instead of searching for a linear sequence of actions, an algorithm decomposes higher-level tasks using a method library until only executable actions remain. On one hand, this allows one to introduce domain knowledge that can speed up the search for a solution through the method library. On the other hand, it creates challenges that go beyond those of classical state-space search. While recent research produced a number of heuristics and novel algorithms that speed up HTN planning, these heuristics are not yet as informative as those available in classical planning algorithms. We investigate whether large language models (LLMs) can generate effective search heuristics for HTN planning, extending the methodology of Corrêa, Pereira, and Seipp (2025) from classical to hierarchical planning. Using the Pytrich planner on six standard total-order HTN benchmark domains, we evaluate heuristics generated by nine LLMs under domain-specific prompting and compare them against the TDG and LMCount domain-independent baselines and the PANDA planner. Our results show that LLM-generated heuristics nearly match the coverage of the best available HTN planner, while substantially reducing search effort on 83% of shared problems.

### [52] [Alternating Target-Path Planning for Scalable Multi-Agent Coordination](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07744v2)
*Yu Kumagai,Keisuke Okumura*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多agent路径规划迭代解耦框架，可迁移至多agent协作规划。

TL;DR: 提出一个迭代细化框架，通过解耦目标分配与路径查找并利用MAPF反馈重新分配，显著提升TAPF问题的可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有CBS方法将目标分配与路径查找紧密耦合，导致计算密集、无法扩展至大规模问题。

Method: 构建迭代细化框架，在给定时间预算内反复求解当前目标分配的MAPF，通过MAPF反馈识别瓶颈智能体并重新分配目标。

Result: 框架能够扩展到远超CBS求解器的规模，同时保持可观的解质量。

Conclusion: 反馈驱动的重新分配循环有效，为实际大规模TAPF提供了可行方案。

中文摘要：并发目标分配和路径查找（TAPF）问题通过要求规划器为智能体分配不同的目标和无冲突路径，扩展了多智能体路径查找（MAPF）。先前关于TAPF的工作完全依赖于基于冲突的搜索（CBS），该方法将目标分配和路径查找紧密耦合，导致计算密集、不可扩展的解决方案。相比之下，我们提出了一个迭代细化框架，将目标分配与路径查找解耦。我们的框架建立在现代、快速、次优的MAPF求解器（如LaCAM）之上。具体而言，在给定的时间预算内，它反复求解当前目标分配的MAPF问题，通过MAPF反馈识别瓶颈智能体，并细化分配。实证结果表明，反馈驱动的重新分配循环是有效的，使我们的框架能够扩展到远超最先进的基于CBS的求解器的范围，同时保持可观的解质量。这代表了向适用于实际场景的大规模TAPF迈出的坚实一步。

Original abstract: The concurrent target assignment and pathfinding (TAPF) problem extends multi-agent pathfinding (MAPF) by asking planners to allocate distinct targets and collision-free paths to agents. Prior work on TAPF has relied exclusively on Conflict-Based Search (CBS), which tightly couples target assignment and pathfinding, resulting in compute-intensive, non-scalable solutions. In contrast, we propose an iterative refinement framework that decouples target assignment from pathfinding. Our framework builds on modern, fast, suboptimal MAPF solvers, such as LaCAM. Specifically, within a given time budget, it repeatedly solves MAPF for the current target assignment, identifies bottleneck agents via MAPF feedback, and refines the assignment. Empirical results show that feedback-driven reassignment loop is effective, enabling our framework to scale well beyond the reach of the state-of-the-art CBS-based solver while maintaining decent solution quality. This represents a solid step toward practical, large scale TAPF suitable for real-world setups.

### [53] [AgentEscapeBench: Evaluating Out-of-Domain Tool-Grounded Reasoning in LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07926v2)
*Zhengkang Guo,Yiyang Li,Lin Qiu,Xiaohua Wang,Jingwen Xv,Dongyu Ru,Xiaoyu Li,Xiaoqing Zheng,Xuezhi Cao,Xunliang Cai*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: LLM agent工具推理benchmark，评估长程依赖与状态跟踪，对agent设计有参考价值。

TL;DR: AgentEscapeBench是一个测试LLM智能体在远程依赖约束下进行工具推理的基准，实验发现性能随依赖深度下降明显，主要失败原因是远程状态追踪和中间结果传播问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM智能体日益依赖外部工具，但缺乏评估其在长距离依赖下工具推理能力的基准。

Method: 设计了密室逃脱风格的基准AgentEscapeBench，包含270个实例和五个难度等级，每个任务定义有向无环依赖图，要求智能体调用真实函数、追踪隐藏状态、传播中间结果并提交答案。

Result: 在16个LLM智能体和人类上的实验表明，随着依赖深度增加性能下降：人类从98.3%降至80.0%，最佳模型从90.0%降至60.0%。轨迹分析显示失败主因是远程状态追踪、线索遵守和中间结果传播的问题。

Conclusion: 当前智能体擅长局部工具使用但在深层上下文依赖上表现不足，AgentEscapeBench可作为诊断测试平台，促进更稳健的通用推理和适应能力的研究。

中文摘要：随着基于大语言模型的智能体越来越依赖外部工具，评估它们在熟悉工作流和短距离交互之外维持工具驱动推理的能力变得重要。我们引入了AgentEscapeBench，一个密室逃脱风格的基准测试，用于测试智能体在明确的远程依赖约束下推断、执行和修正新型工具使用程序的能力。每个任务定义了一个工具和物品上的有向无环依赖图，要求智能体调用真实的外部函数，追踪逐步揭示的隐藏状态，传播中间结果，并提交一个可确定性验证的最终答案。AgentEscapeBench包含270个实例，覆盖五个难度等级，并支持全自动评估。使用16个LLM智能体和人类参与者进行的实验表明，随着依赖深度的增加，性能急剧下降：人类在难度5时的成功率为98.3%，到难度25时降至80.0%；而最佳模型从90.0%降至60.0%。轨迹分析将模型失败主要归因于远程状态追踪、线索遵守和中间结果传播的崩溃。这些发现表明，当前的智能体通常能处理局部工具使用，但在深层上下文依赖方面仍然挣扎。我们希望AgentEscapeBench能够作为一个诊断测试平台，用于衡量当前智能体的能力，并为未来训练更稳健的通用推理、行动和适应能力提供信息。

Original abstract: As LLM-based agents increasingly rely on external tools, it is important to evaluate their ability to sustain tool-grounded reasoning beyond familiar workflows and short-range interactions. We introduce AgentEscapeBench, an escape-room-style benchmark that tests whether agents can infer, execute, and revise novel tool-use procedures under explicit long-range dependency constraints. Each task defines a directed acyclic dependency graph over tools and items, requiring agents to invoke real external functions, track hidden state revealed incrementally, propagate intermediate results, and submit a deterministically verifiable final answer. AgentEscapeBench includes 270 instances across five difficulty tiers and supports fully automated evaluation. Experiments with sixteen LLM agents and human participants show that performance drops sharply as dependency depth increases: humans decline from 98.3% success at difficulty-5 to 80.0% at difficulty-25, while the best model drops from 90.0% to 60.0%. Trajectory analysis attributes model failures mainly to breakdowns in long-range state tracking, clue adherence, and intermediate-result propagation. These findings suggest that current agents can often handle local tool use but still struggle with deep contextual dependencies. We hope AgentEscapeBench can serve as a diagnostic testbed for measuring current agent capabilities and informing future training efforts toward more robust general-purpose reasoning, action, and adaptation.

</details>


### [54] [TraceFix: Repairing Agent Coordination Protocols with TLA+ Counterexamples](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07935v1)
*Shuren Xia,Qiwei Li,Taqiya Ehsan,Jorge Ortiz*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 用TLA+验证修复多agent协调协议，涉及协议合成与迭代修复，对coding agent调试有启发。

TL;DR: TraceFix通过TLA+验证确保多智能体协议正确性，显著提升任务完成率并减少死锁。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM多智能体协调缺乏形式化验证，导致协议容易出错且难以保证正确性。

Method: 从任务描述合成协议拓扑，生成PlusCal逻辑并用TLC模型检查器迭代修复，验证后编译为系统提示，运行时监控拓扑合规。

Result: 48个任务全部通过验证，62.5%一次性通过，最多4次修复；运行时比较中拓扑监控执行平均任务完成率89.4%，验证协议将死锁/活锁从31.1%降至14.1%。

Conclusion: 验证优先的流水线能有效提高多智能体协调的可靠性和性能，尤其在模型能力下降时表现出更强的鲁棒性。

中文摘要：我们提出了TraceFix，一种用于大语言模型多智能体协调的验证优先流水线。智能体从任务描述中合成协议拓扑作为结构化中间表示，生成PlusCal协调逻辑，并利用TLA+模型检查器（TLC）的反例迭代修复协议，直到验证成功。验证后的过程体被编译为每个智能体的系统提示，并在运行时监控下执行，拒绝超出拓扑的协调操作。在涵盖16个场景类别的48个任务上，所有任务都达到了完全TLC验证；62.5%首次尝试即通过，没有一个需要超过四次修复迭代。状态空间跨越六个数量级，但每个任务的验证都在60秒内完成。一项3456次运行的运行时比较表明，拓扑监控执行实现了最高的任务完成度（平均89.4%，完全完成81.5%），并且当模型能力降低时，使用经过验证的协议的运行时退化速度大约是仅提示和仅聊天基线的一半。在固定运行时的配对消融研究中，TLC验证的协议将死锁/活锁从31.1%降至14.1%，在故障注入下分离最大。

Original abstract: We present TraceFix, a verification-first pipeline for Large Language Model (LLM) multi-agent coordination. An agent synthesizes a protocol topology as a structured intermediate representation (IR) from a task description, generates PlusCal coordination logic, and iteratively repairs the protocol using counterexamples from the TLA+ model checker (TLC) until verification succeeds. Verified process bodies are compiled into per-agent system prompts and executed under a runtime monitor that rejects out-of-topology coordination operations. On 48 tasks spanning 16 scenario families, all tasks reach full TLC verification; 62.5% pass on the first attempt and none requires more than four repair iterations. State spaces span six orders of magnitude yet verification completes in under 60 s for every task. A 3,456-run runtime comparison shows that topology-monitored execution achieves the highest task completion (89.4% average, 81.5% full) and that runtimes using the verified protocol degrade at roughly half the rate of prompt-only and chat-only baselines when model capability is reduced. A paired ablation under a fixed runtime shows that TLC-verified protocols cut deadlock/livelock (DL/LL) from 31.1% to 14.1%, with the largest separation under fault injection.

*Joseph Cotnareanu,Chiara Roverato,Han Zhou,Didier Chetelat,Yingxue Zhang,Mark Coates*

Main category: cs.AI

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出概率溯因常识推理框架PACS，使用LLM和形式求解器采样证明作为个体常识信念的观测，并聚合结论。

Result: PACS在多个基准测试上优于思维链、先前神经符号方法和搜索方法。

Conclusion: 通过显式建模常识信念的个体差异，概率框架能有效提升LLM在溯因常识推理上的表现。

中文摘要：最近提升大语言模型推理能力的努力集中在将形式逻辑求解器整合到神经符号框架中。一个关键挑战是形式求解器缺乏常识性世界知识，这使它们无法进行人类认为显而易见的推理步骤。先前的方法通过使用LLM提供缺失的常识性假设来解决这个问题，但这些方法隐含地假设对这些常识事实存在普遍共识。实际上，常识性信念因人而异。我们提出了一个用于溯因常识推理的概率框架，明确建模这种变异，旨在确定大多数人是否会判断一个陈述为真或假。我们引入了概率溯因常识推理（PACS），一种新颖的算法，它使用LLM和形式求解器采样证明作为个人不同常识信念的观测，并聚合这些样本中的结论。实验上，PACS在多个基准测试中优于思维链推理、先前的神经符号方法和基于搜索的方法。

Original abstract: Recent efforts to improve the reasoning abilities of Large Language Models (LLMs) have focused on integrating formal logic solvers within neurosymbolic frameworks. A key challenge is that formal solvers lack commonsense world knowledge, preventing them from making reasoning steps that humans find obvious. Prior methods address this by using LLMs to supply missing commonsense assumptions, but these approaches implicitly assume universal agreement on such commonsense facts. In reality, commonsense beliefs vary across individuals. We propose a probabilistic framework for abductive commonsense reasoning that explicitly models this variation, aiming to determine whether most people would judge a statement as true or false. We introduce Probabilistic Abductive CommonSense (PACS), a novel algorithm that uses an LLM and a formal solver to sample proofs as observations of individuals' distinct commonsense beliefs, and aggregates conclusions across these samples. Empirically, PACS outperforms chain-of-thought reasoning, prior neurosymbolic methods, and search-based approaches across multiple benchmarks.

*Haoyang Su,Ying Wen*

Selection reason: 直接研究CLI agent学习，提出结构化动作信用分配方法A³，与代码优化agent高度相关。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CLI代理面临两个主要瓶颈：从部分观察中识别代码库证据，以及稀疏奖励在长轨迹中的信用分配。现有RL方法未充分利用CLI动作的结构化属性。

Method: 提出σ-Reveal（推理时选择token预算化上下文）和A^3（基于AST动作子链残差和树级轨迹边际的回合级优势分配），并构建ShellOps数据集。

中文摘要：命令行界面（CLI）代理正成为在不断演变的文件系统、可执行命令行程序和在线执行反馈中实现代理-计算机交互的一种实用范式。最近的工作使用强化学习（RL）从可验证的任务反馈中学习这些交互能力，但很少有方法利用CLI操作的原生结构化属性作为学习信号。除了这种未被充分利用的动作结构，CLI学习还为编码代理带来了两个瓶颈。首先，代理必须从部分观察中识别大型代码库中与任务相关的证据。其次，稀疏的终端奖励必须分配给构成长多轮轨迹的动作。我们通过shell驱动的信息提取和文件编辑任务来研究这些瓶颈。对于选择性观察，我们引入了σ-Reveal，一种推理时机制，为同一CLI选择标记预算化的上下文。对于信用分配，我们提出了动作优势分配（A^3），一种本体的代理RL方法，它保留了标准代理RL的算法复杂性。A^3从回合级相对反馈、基于抽象语法树（AST）的动作子链残差和树级轨迹边际中构建回合级优势。为了进一步评估这个问题设置，我们构建了ShellOps，一个涵盖仓库环境中CLI任务的可验证数据集套件。

Original abstract: Command line interface (CLI) agents are emerging as a practical paradigm for agent-computer interaction over evolving filesystems, executable command line programs, and online execution feedback. Recent work has used reinforcement learning (RL) to learn these interaction abilities from verifiable task feedback, yet few methods exploit the native structured attributes of CLI actions as learning signals. Beyond this underused action structure, CLI learning also couples two bottlenecks for coding agents. First, the agent must identify task-relevant evidence in a large codebase from partial observations. Second, sparse terminal rewards must be assigned to the actions that shape a long multi-turn trajectory. We study these bottlenecks through shell-driven information extraction and file editing tasks. For selective observation, we introduce $σ$-Reveal, an inference-time mechanism that selects token-budgeted context for the same CLI. For credit assignment, we propose Action Advantage Assignment ($\mathrm{A}^3$), a native agentic RL method that preserves the algorithmic complexity of standard agentic RL. $\mathrm{A}^3$ constructs turn-level advantages from episode-level relative feedback, abstract syntax tree (AST) based action sub-chain residuals, and tree-level trajectory margins. To further evaluate this problem setting, we construct ShellOps, a verifiable dataset suite covering CLI tasks in repository environments.

### [57] [MemQ: Integrating Q-Learning into Self-Evolving Memory Agents over Provenance DAGs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08374v3)
*Junwei Liao,Haoting Shi,Ruiwen Zhou,Jiaqian Wang,Shengtao Zhang,Wei Zhang,Ying Wen,Zhiyu Li,Feiyu Xiong,Bo Tang,Weinan Zhang,Muning Wen*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出基于Q-learning的自演化记忆agent，直接适用于coding agent记忆管理。

TL;DR: MemQ通过TD(λ)资格迹在记忆溯源DAG中反向传播信用，显著提升了LLM代理在多步任务上的情景记忆表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM代理的情景记忆方法独立处理每个记忆，忽略了记忆之间的依赖链，导致在多步任务中检索质量不佳。

Method: 提出MemQ，将TD(λ)资格迹应用于记忆Q值，通过记录记忆创建时检索关系的溯源DAG，按DAG深度衰减信用权重，形式化为Exogenous-Context MDP。

Result: 在六个基准测试中，MemQ在泛化和运行时学习上均取得最高成功率，多步任务提升达+5.7个百分点，单步分类提升仅+0.77个百分点。

Conclusion: MemQ有效利用记忆依赖链，在多种复杂任务中提升LLM代理性能，参数γ和λ可依据EC-MDP结构进行原则性选择。

中文摘要：情景记忆使LLM代理能够积累和检索经验，但当前的方法独立处理每个记忆，即孤立地评估检索质量，而不考虑记忆通过其使得未来记忆得以创建的依赖链。我们引入了MemQ，它将TD($\lambda$)资格迹应用于记忆Q值，通过一个记录每个新记忆创建时检索了哪些记忆的溯源有向无环图（DAG）向后传播信用。信用权重以$(\gamma\lambda)^d$随DAG深度$d$衰减，用结构接近度取代时间距离。我们将该设定形式化为一个外生上下文MDP（Exogenous-Context MDP），其分解转换将外生任务流与内生记忆存储解耦。在六个基准测试中，涵盖操作系统交互、函数调用、代码生成、多模态推理、具身推理和专家级问答，MemQ在泛化评估和运行时学习中均取得了所有六个基准的最高成功率，其中在多步任务（产生深度且相关的溯源链）上增益最大（最高+5.7个百分点），在单步分类（单步更新已足够）上增益最小（+0.77个百分点）。我们进一步研究了$\gamma$和$\lambda$如何与EC-MDP结构交互，为参数选择和未来研究提供了原则性指导。代码可在https://github.com/jwliao-ai/MemQ获取。

Original abstract: Episodic memory allows LLM agents to accumulate and retrieve experience, but current methods treat each memory independently, i.e., evaluating retrieval quality in isolation without accounting for the dependency chains through which memories enable the creation of future memories. We introduce MemQ, which applies TD($λ$) eligibility traces to memory Q-values, propagating credit backward through a provenance DAG that records which memories were retrieved when each new memory was created. Credit weight decays as $(γλ)^d$ with DAG depth $d$, replacing temporal distance with structural proximity. We formalize the setting as an Exogenous-Context MDP, whose factored transition decouples the exogenous task stream from the endogenous memory store. Across six benchmarks, spanning OS interaction, function calling, code generation, multimodal reasoning, embodied reasoning, and expert-level QA, MemQ achieves the highest success rate on all six in generalization evaluation and runtime learning, with gains largest on multi-step tasks that produce deep and relevant provenance chains (up to +5.7~pp) and smallest on single-step classification (+0.77~pp) where single-step updates already suffice. We further study how $γ$ and $λ$ interact with the EC-MDP structure, providing principled guidance for parameter selection and future research. Code is available at https://github.com/jwliao-ai/MemQ.

### [58] [SkillLens: Adaptive Multi-Granularity Skill Reuse for Cost-Efficient LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08386v1)
*Yongliang Miao,Ziyang Yu,Liang Zhao,Bowen Zhu,Hasibul Haque*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出技能库的层次化复用框架，适用于LLM智能体的规划与记忆重用，可直接迁移至编码智能体的技能管理。

TL;DR: 提出SkillLens，一种分层技能演化框架，通过混合粒度检索和动态验证机制，在保持低成本的同时提升LLM代理的任务性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有技能库将技能视为扁平、单一分辨率的提示块，导致注入粗粒度技能可能引入无关上下文，而重写整个技能成本高昂，需要在相关性和成本之间进行权衡。

Method: 构建四层技能图（策略、战略、程序、原语），通过语义检索种子、度修正随机游走扩展，并利用验证器对每个访问单元进行接受、分解、重写或跳过决策，同时通过演化更新不断优化技能和验证器。

Result: 在MuLocbench上缺陷定位Acc@1提升6.31个百分点，在ALFWorld上代理成功率从45.00%提升至51.31%，一致优于强基线。

Conclusion: 混合粒度自适应在稀疏不匹配假设下成本次线性，演化规则单调改进验证目标至局部最优，验证了SkillLens在技能重用和自适应方面的有效性。

中文摘要：技能库已成为LLM代理跨任务重用程序性经验的一种实用方式。然而，现有系统通常将技能视为扁平的、单一分辨率的提示块。这造成了相关性和成本之间的紧张关系：注入粗粒度技能可能引入不相关或误导性的上下文，而重写整个技能成本高昂且往往不必要。我们提出SkillLens，一种分层技能演化框架，将技能组织成策略、战略、程序和原语的四层图，并以混合粒度进行检索。给定一个任务，SkillLens首先检索语义相关的技能种子，通过度修正随机游走在技能图上扩展它们，然后使用验证器决定每个访问单元应被接受、分解、重写还是跳过。这使得代理能够直接重用兼容的子技能，同时仅适应局部不匹配的组件。为了随时间改进系统，SkillLens进一步细化多粒度技能和验证器，以改进其路由决策。我们提供了理论分析，表明在稀疏不匹配假设下，混合粒度自适应产生次线性成本，并且演化更新规则单调地改进验证目标直到局部最优。在MuLocbench和ALFWorld上，SkillLens持续优于强技能基线，在缺陷定位上实现了高达6.31个百分点的Acc@1增益，并将代理成功率从45.00%提升至51.31%。

Original abstract: Skill libraries have become a practical way for LLM agents to reuse procedural experience across tasks. However, existing systems typically treat skills as flat, single-resolution prompt blocks. This creates a tension between relevance and cost: injecting coarse skills can introduce irrelevant or misleading context, while rewriting entire skills is expensive and often unnecessary. We propose SkillLens, a hierarchical skill-evolution framework that organizes skills into a four-layer graph of policies, strategies, procedures, and primitives, and retrieves them at mixed granularity. Given a task, SkillLens first retrieves semantically relevant skill seeds, expands them through degree-corrected random walk over the skill graph, and then uses a verifier to decide whether each visited unit should be accepted, decomposed, rewritten, or skipped. This enables the agent to reuse compatible subskills directly while adapting only locally mismatched components. To improve the system over time, SkillLens further refines multi-granularity skills and verifier in order to improve its routing decisions. We provide theoretical analysis showing that mixed-granularity adaptation incurs sublinear cost under sparse mismatch assumptions and that the evolutionary update rule monotonically improves the validation objective until a local optimum. Across MuLocbench and ALFWorld, SkillLens consistently improves over strong skill-based baselines, achieving up to a 6.31 percentage-point Acc@1 gain for bug localization and raising agent success rate from 45.00% to 51.31%.

### [59] [CoCoDA: Co-evolving Compositional DAG for Tool-Augmented Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08399v1)

TL;DR: CoCoDA通过组合代码DAG共同演化规划器和工具库，实现检索成本亚线性、库规模无关的提示成本，并在多个基准上使小模型超越大模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工具使用方法中，工具库增长导致检索成本线性增加且忽视代码的组合结构，亟需一种能同时演化规划器和工具库并保持检索高效的框架。

Method: CoCoDA构建组合代码DAG，节点为工具并存储类型签名、规范、示例；推理时通过类型化DAG检索逐步剪枝、排序、过滤、消除歧义；训练时将成功轨迹压缩为复合工具并用DAG诱导奖励更新规划器。

Result: 在GSM8K、MATH等基准上，8B学生模型匹配或超过32B教师模型，并显著优于现有工具使用和库学习方法。

Conclusion: CoCoDA有效实现了规划器与工具库的协同演化，在保持固定上下文预算的同时提升小模型能力，理论分析和实验均验证其优势。

中文摘要：工具增强的语言模型可以通过外部可执行技能扩展小型语言模型，但扩展工具库带来了一个耦合挑战：库必须随着规划器一起演化，因为新的可重用子程序会出现，同时从不断增长的库中检索必须保持在固定的上下文预算内。现有的工具使用和技能库方法通常将工具视为平坦或文本索引的记忆，导致提示成本随库大小增长，并掩盖了可执行代码的类型化、组合结构。我们提出了CoCoDA，一个通过单一代码原生结构（即组合代码DAG）共同演化规划器和工具库的框架。节点是原始或复合工具，边编码调用依赖，每个节点存储类型签名、描述、前置/后置条件规范和工作示例。在推理时，类型化DAG检索通过符号签名统一剪枝候选，按描述排序，按行为规范过滤，并用示例消除歧义，将昂贵的上下文物化保持在逐渐变小的候选集上。在训练时，成功的轨迹被折叠成验证过的复合工具，同时通过一个由DAG诱导的奖励来更新规划器，该奖励根据原始扩展大小对复合工具进行信用分配。我们提供了理论结果，展示了检索成本降低、亚线性检索时间、在形状奖励下的组合优势、在保守更新下的单调共同演化以及DAG良好形式。在数学推理、表格分析和代码任务基准上，CoCoDA使一个8B学生模型在GSM8K和MATH上匹配或超过32B教师模型，并持续优于强工具使用和库学习基线。

Original abstract: Tool-augmented language models can extend small language models with external executable skills, but scaling the tool library creates a coupled challenge: the library must evolve with the planner as new reusable subroutines emerge, while retrieval from the growing library must remain within a fixed context budget. Existing tool-use and skill-library methods typically treat tools as flat or text-indexed memories, causing prompt cost to grow with library size and obscuring the typed, compositional structure of executable code. We propose CoCoDA, a framework that co-evolves the planner and tool library through a single code-native structure: a compositional code DAG. Nodes are primitive or composite tools, edges encode invocation dependencies, and each node stores a typed signature, description, pre/post-condition specification, and worked examples. At inference time, Typed DAG Retrieval prunes candidates by symbolic signature unification, ranks survivors by descriptions, filters them by behavioral specifications, and disambiguates with examples, keeping expensive context materialization on progressively smaller candidate sets. At training time, successful trajectories are folded into validated composite tools, while the planner is updated with a DAG-induced reward that credits composites by their primitive expansion size. We provide theoretical results showing retrieval cost reduction, sublinear retrieval time, compositional advantage under the shaped reward, monotone co-evolution under conservative updates, and DAG well-formedness. Across mathematical reasoning, tabular analysis, and code task benchmarks, CoCoDA enables an 8B student to match or exceed a 32B teacher on GSM8K and MATH and consistently improves over strong tool-use and library-learning baselines.

</details>


### [60] [Playing games with knowledge: AI-Induced delusions need game theoretic interventions](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08409v1)
*Will Beaumaster,Paul Schrater*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 从博弈论角度分析AI诱导的认知固化，提出中介干预和信念版本管理，对智能体安全通信有启发。

TL;DR: 通过认识论中介干预，在对话AI中打破谄媚导致的混合均衡，实现分离均衡并大幅降低信念螺旋率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对话AI的谄媚特性会导致用户形成病态确定的错误信念，即使是理性智能体也难以避免。现有研究多聚焦于模型对齐，但作者认为问题根源在于用户与AI之间的战略通信环境设计不当，从而引发系统性认知风险。

Method: 将对话AI与用户的交互形式化为Crawford-Sobel廉价谈话博弈，揭示其混合均衡缺陷。提出认识论中介机制，通过引入认识论摩擦（成本信号）迫使不同用户类型（成长寻求者与验证寻求者）暴露真实身份，并设计信念版本控制系统（类似git）存储健康信念并在检测到验证寻求行为时回滚。

Result: 模拟测试表明，认识论中介干预实现了分离均衡，相比基线策略将信念螺旋发生率降低了48倍，同时满足学习保留标准，验证了干预的有效性。

Conclusion: AI的认识论安全性本质上是战略信息环境设计问题，而非简单的模型对齐。通过引入认识论摩擦和信念版本控制，可以系统性地打破谄媚导致的认知陷阱，为构建更可靠的对话AI提供新范式。

中文摘要：对话式AI作为知识接口存在一个根本缺陷：谄媚的聊天机器人即使在理性智能体中也诱导认识论固化和妄想信念螺旋。我们认为问题并非源于AI模型本身，而是植根于从用户驱动的知识搜索到用户与代理进行战略性、重复性通信的范式转变的系统性后果。我们将该问题形式化为一个Crawford-Sobel廉价谈话博弈，其中无成本的用户信号导致了一个混合均衡。针对用户满意度优化的代理会产生谄媚策略，为具有相反认识论激励的用户类型提供相同的强化：探索性的“成长寻求者”（θ_G）和确认性的“验证寻求者”（θ_V）。在重复博弈下，这种识别失败造成了一个协调陷阱——类似于囚徒困境——其中局部理性的反馈循环将用户驱动至病态确定的错误信念。我们提出一种推理时机制设计干预措施，称为认识论中介，通过引入一个成本信号（认识论摩擦）打破这一混合均衡，迫使用户基于处理阻力的不对称认知成本进行类型揭示。一个关键贡献是信念版本控制，一种受git启发的认识论元记忆系统，存储健康信念并在检测到验证寻求阻力时进行回滚。在模拟中，该干预实现了分离均衡，螺旋率差异达到48倍，同时通过了学习保留标准，这表明AI中的认识论安全性根本上是战略信息环境设计问题，而非简单的模型对齐。

Original abstract: Conversational AI has a fundamental flaw as a knowledge interface: sycophantic chatbots induce epistemic entrenchment and delusional belief spirals even in rational agents. We propose the problem does not stem from the AI model, rooted instead in a systemic consequence of the paradigm shift from user-driven knowledge search to users and agents engaged in strategic, repeated-play communication. We formalize the problem as a Crawford-Sobel cheap talk game, where costless user signals induce a pooling equilibrium. Agents optimized for user satisfaction produce sycophantic strategies that provide identical reinforcement across user types with opposite epistemic incentives: exploratory ``Growth-seekers'' ($θ_G$) and confirmatory ``Validation-seekers'' ($θ_V$). Under repeated play, this identification failure creates a coordination trap -- analogous to a Prisoner's Dilemma -- where locally rational feedback loops drive users toward pathologically certain false beliefs. We propose an inference-time mechanism design intervention called an Epistemic Mediator that breaks this pooling equilibrium by introducing a costly signal (epistemic friction), forcing type revelation based on users' asymmetric cognitive costs for processing resistance. A key contribution is Belief Versioning, a git-inspired epistemic meta-memory system that stores healthy beliefs and rollbacks when validation-seeking resistance is detected. In simulation, this intervention achieves a separating equilibrium achieving a $48\times$ differential in spiral rates while passing a learning preservation criterion), evidence that epistemic safety in AI is fundamentally a problem of strategic information environment design rather than simple model alignment.

</details>


### [61] [The Attacker in the Mirror: Breaking Self-Consistency in Safety via Anchored Bipolicy Self-Play](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08427v1)
*Gabriele La Malfa,Emanuele La Malfa,Saar Cohen,Jie M. Zhang,Michael Luck,Michael Wooldridge,Elizabeth Black*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出锚定双策略自对弈提升智能体鲁棒性，其对抗训练框架可迁移至代码智能体安全。

TL;DR: 提出锚定双策略自对抗，通过冻结基础模型并训练角色特定LoRA适配器，解决了自对抗中攻击者与防御者参数共享导致的动态坍缩问题，实现了高效且鲁棒的安全对齐。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的自对抗红队方法虽能改善AI安全性，但攻击者与防御者共享同一模型参数导致动态坍缩为自一致性，攻击无法施加有效对抗压力，且可达的纳什均衡包含无意义策略，限制了实际应用。

Method: 提出锚定双策略自对抗（Anchored Bipolicy Self-Play），在冻结的基础模型之上为攻击者和防御者分别训练角色特定的LoRA适配器，实现明确的角色分离，保持优化稳定性同时保留对抗压力。

Result: 在Qwen2.5-{3B,7B,14B}-IT模型上，该方法相比自对抗微调模型在安全性基准上一致改进，参数效率提升高达100倍，且不损失推理能力。交叉博弈实验表明攻击者和防御者模型在对抗防御和安全性上优于自对抗。

Conclusion: 锚定双策略自对抗通过角色分离的LoRA适配器有效解决了自对抗的局限性，实现了高效、鲁棒的安全对齐，为AI安全训练提供了新范式。

中文摘要：自对抗红队是一种改进AI安全性的已有方法，其中同一模型的不同实例在零和博弈中扮演攻击者和防御者的角色，即攻击者试图越狱防御者；如果自对抗收敛到纳什均衡，则该模型保证在博弈设定内安全响应。尽管由于两个角色使用相同模型而强制进行的参数共享提高了稳定性和性能，但它引入了基本的理论和架构限制。我们表明，可达到的纳什均衡集合对应于广泛的行为类别，包括琐碎的始终拒绝策略和类似神谕的防御者，从而限制了实际适用性。然后我们证明，当攻击者和防御者共享并更新相同的基础模型时，动态会坍缩为自一致性，因此攻击不会对防御者施加对抗压力。作为回应，我们提出了锚定双策略自对抗（Anchored Bipolicy Self-Play），它在冻结的基础模型之上训练不同的角色特定LoRA适配器，从而在保持稳定优化的同时，通过明确的角色分离保留对抗压力。与标准自对抗相比，我们展示了相比微调高达100倍的参数效率提升，以及与自对抗微调模型相比一致的安全性改进。我们在广泛使用的安全基准测试上评估了Qwen2.5-{3B, 7B, 14B}-IT模型，显示出改进的鲁棒性而不损失推理能力。交叉博弈实验进一步表明，我们的攻击者和防御者模型在对抗防御和安全性方面优于自对抗。

Original abstract: Self-play red team is an established approach to improving AI safety in which different instances of the same model play attacker and defender roles in a zero-sum game, i.e., where the attacker tries to jailbreak the defender; if self-play converges to a Nash equilibrium, the model is guaranteed to respond safely within the settings of the game. Although the parameter sharing enforced by the use of the same model for the two roles improves stability and performance, it introduces fundamental theoretical and architectural limitations. We show that the set of Nash equilibria that can be reached corresponds to a broad class of behaviours that includes trivial always refuse strategies and oracle-like defenders, thus limiting practical applicability. We then show that when attacker and defender share and update the same base model, the dynamics collapse to self-consistency, so that attacks do not enforce adversarial pressure on the defender. In response, we propose Anchored Bipolicy Self-Play, which trains distinct role-specific LoRA adapters on top of a frozen base model, thereby maintaining stable optimisation while preserving adversarial pressure through explicit role separation. In relation to standard self-play, we show up to 100x greater parameter efficiency than finetuning and consistent improvements in safety compared to self-play fine-tuned models. We evaluate on Qwen2.5-{3B, 7B,14B}-IT models across widely used safety benchmarks, showing improved robustness without loss of reasoning ability. Cross-play experiments further show that our attacker and defender models are superior to self-play in terms of adversarial defence and safety.

</details>


### [62] [Behavioral Determinants of Deployed AI Agents in Social Networks: A Multi-Factor Study of Personality, Model, and Guardrail Specification](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08463v2)
*Sarah Wilson,Diem Linh Dang,Usman Ali Moazzam,Shan Ye,Gail Kaiser*

TL;DR: 本文通过多因素实证研究，发现个性规范是影响AI代理涌现社会行为的主要因素，而模型骨干和操作规则具有次要但显著的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在Molbook社交网络上部署13个OpenClaw代理，系统性地变化个性规范、LLM模型骨干和操作规则三个自变量，通过一周观察收集行为、语言和社交指标进行分析。

Result: 个性规范主导行为差异（如回复长度），模型骨干和操作规则影响修辞风格和话题参与广度。

Conclusion: 该研究为多Agent社交系统提供了实证证据，并为设计用于真实社会环境的代理提供了实践指导。

中文摘要：自主AI代理越来越多地部署在开放的社会环境中，但其配置规范与涌现的社会行为之间的关系仍然知之甚少。我们进行了一项受控的多因素实证研究，其中13个OpenClaw代理被部署在Molbook（一个为AI代理构建的类Reddit社交网络）上，系统性地变化了三个自变量：（1）个性规范，（2）底层LLM模型骨干，以及（3）操作规则和记忆配置。一个默认控制代理提供了行为基线。在一周的观察窗口内，每个代理大约有400个自主会话，我们收集了行为、语言和社交指标，以评估配置层如何预测涌现的社会行为。我们发现个性规范是主导的行为杠杆，导致代理之间回复长度的巨大差异，而模型骨干和操作规则对修辞风格和话题参与广度产生了更温和但仍显著的影响。我们的研究结果为新兴的关于部署的多Agent社交系统的文献提供了实证证据，并为设计用于真实社交环境中的协作或监控任务的代理提供了实践指导。

Original abstract: Autonomous AI agents are increasingly deployed in open social environments, yet the relationship between their configuration specifications and their emergent social behavior remains poorly understood. We present a controlled, multi-factor empirical study in which thirteen OpenClaw agents are deployed on Moltbook -- a Reddit-like social network built for AI agents -- across three systematically varied independent variables: (1) personality specification, (2) underlying LLM model backbone, and (3) operational rules and memory configuration. A default control agent provides a behavioral baseline. Over a one-week observation window spanning approximately 400 autonomous sessions per agent, we collect behavioral, linguistic, and social metrics to assess how configuration layers predict emergent social behavior. We find that personality specification is the dominant behavioral lever, producing a massive spread in response length across agents, while model backbone and operational rules drive more moderate but still meaningful effects on rhetorical style and topic engagement breadth. Our findings contribute empirical evidence to the emerging literature on deployed multi-agent social systems and offer practical guidance for designing agents intended for collaborative or monitoring tasks in real social environments.

### [63] [Mid-Training with Self-Generated Data Improves Reinforcement Learning in Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08472v1)
*Aswin RRV,Jacob Dineen,Divij Handa,Mihir Parmar,Ben Zhou,Swaroop Mishra,Chitta Baral*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 自生成数据中训练改进RL，可用于agent训练阶段。

TL;DR: 在RL训练前使用多样化的自生成数据进行中期训练，可以显著提升LLM在数学推理和其他OOD任务上的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: RL在LLM中的有效性受限于训练数据的多样性和范围，尤其是推理问题有多种解法，而数据中若只包含少量解法会限制RL效果。

Method: 采用基于波利亚问题解决方法的引导式框架，为每个问题生成多个正确答案变体，进行中期微调，然后进行RL训练。

Result: 经过中期训练初始化的RL模型在多个数学推理基准以及代码生成、叙事推理等OOD任务上均取得一致改进。

Conclusion: 通过自生成数据学习多种问题解决方法的语言模型能够提升后续RL训练的效果。

中文摘要：强化学习在大型语言模型中的有效性取决于RL之前和期间所用数据的性质和多样性。特别是，推理问题通常可以通过依赖于不同推理形式的多种方法来解决，而训练数据中仅限于这些方法的有限范围可能会限制RL的有效性。受此启发，我们研究在RL训练之前的中期训练中使用多样化的自生成数据。具体而言，我们采用基于乔治·波利亚问题解决方法的引导式数据生成框架，为训练数据中的每个问题生成正确答案的多个变体，然后进行微调。我们首先从理论上解释了中期训练如何改善RL，并说明了策略梯度更新如何激励组合多种方法。然后我们通过实验证明，使用我们的中期训练数据初始化的RL训练模型在各种数学推理基准以及其他OOD任务（如代码生成和叙事推理）中取得了一致的改进。总体而言，我们的研究表明，通过自生成数据学习多种问题解决方法的语言模型有助于后续的RL训练。

Original abstract: The effectiveness of Reinforcement Learning (RL) in Large Language Models (LLMs) depends on the nature and diversity of the data used before and during RL. In particular, reasoning problems can often be approached in multiple ways that rely on different forms of reasoning, and exposure to only a limited range of such approaches in the training data may limit the effectiveness of RL. Motivated by this, we investigate using diverse self-generated data during mid-training as an intermediate step before RL training. Specifically, we adopt a bootstrapped data-generation framework guided by George Polya's problem-solving approaches for generating multiple variants of correct answers for each question in the training data, and then perform fine-tuning. We first provide a theoretical perspective on how mid-training on such data improves RL and explain how policy-gradient updates can incentivize combining multiple approaches. We then empirically demonstrate that RL-trained models initialized with our mid-training data achieve consistent improvements across various mathematical reasoning benchmarks and other OOD tasks like code generation and narrative reasoning. Overall, our investigative study shows that a language model learning multiple problem-solving approaches, through self-generated data helps subsequent RL.

### [64] [Latent Personality Alignment: Improving Harmlessness Without Mentioning Harms](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08496v1)
*Linh Le,David Williams-King,Mohamed Amine Merzouk,Aton Kamanda,Adam Oberman*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 潜在人格对齐提升鲁棒性，通用agent安全对齐方法。

TL;DR: 提出一种仅需少量特质样本的人格对齐方法，无需有害示例即可实现高效且泛化能力强的鲁棒防御。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有鲁棒性方法依赖大量有害数据，且难以应对新攻击和分布变化，效率低且泛化差。

Method: 使用少于100个抽象人格特质语句进行训练，结合潜在对抗训练实现对齐。

Result: 攻击成功率与基于15万+示例的方法相当，误分类率降低2.6倍，且保持高实用性。

Conclusion: 人格对齐为低成本的鲁棒防御提供了可行方案，具有更好的泛化性和样本效率。

中文摘要：当前大型语言模型的对抗鲁棒性方法需要大量有害提示数据集（数千到数十万个示例），但仍然容易受到新的攻击向量和分布变化的影响。我们提出潜在人格对齐（LPA），一种样本高效的防御方法，通过训练模型学习抽象人格特质而非特定有害行为来实现鲁棒性。使用少于100个特质陈述和潜在对抗训练，LPA在攻击成功率上达到了与使用15万+示例训练的方法相当的水平，同时保持了更优的实用性。关键的是，LPA对未见过的攻击分布具有更好的泛化能力，在六个危害基准上将误分类率降低了2.6倍——且在训练过程中从未见过有害示例。我们的结果表明，基于人格的对齐提供了一种以最小成本构建鲁棒防御的原则性方法。

Original abstract: Current adversarial robustness methods for large language models require extensive datasets of harmful prompts (thousands to hundreds of thousands of examples), yet remain vulnerable to novel attack vectors and distributional shifts. We propose Latent Personality Alignment (LPA), a sample-efficient defense that achieves robustness by training models on abstract personality traits rather than specific harmful behaviors. Using fewer than 100 trait statements and latent adversarial training, LPA achieves comparable attack success rates to methods trained on 150k+ examples, while maintaining superior utility. Critically, LPA generalizes better to unseen attack distributions, reducing misclassification rates by 2.6x compared to baseline across six harm benchmarks -- without ever seeing harmful examples during training. Our results demonstrate that personality-based alignment offers a principled approach to building robust defenses with minimal cost.

</details>


### [65] [Results and Retrospective Analysis of the CODS 2025 AssetOpsBench Challenge](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08518v1)
*Dhaval Patel,Chathurangi Shyalika,Suryanarayana Reddy Yarrabothula,Ling Yue,Shuxin Lin,Nianjun Zhou,James Rayfield*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 多agent编排竞赛回顾，分析设计模式，对agent架构有启发

TL;DR: 该研究通过多源数据分析CODS 2025挑战赛，揭示了公共与隐藏评估在规划与执行任务中的差异，指出成功方法更注重护栏改进而非新架构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解竞争排行榜的实际衡量内容、隐藏评估如何改变结论以及哪些设计模式被奖励，从而为未来竞赛设计提供见解。

Method: 结合最终排名表、服务器日志、团队注册数据、最佳提交导出、组织者报告、系统论文和规划跟踪源代码，进行多维度分析。

Result: 五个关键发现：1）规划排行榜饱和于72.73%；2）隐藏评估下执行分数与公共分数负相关（r=-0.13），部分系统从45.45%提升至63.64%；3）tmatch项对综合分数贡献微小（≤0.05）；4）多数注册团队实际活跃比例低；5）成功执行方法集中于响应选择、污染清理等护栏改进。

Conclusion: 这些发现识别了评估奖励的行为，激励未来竞赛采用规模感知复合分数、技能水平诊断和版本化工件发布。

中文摘要：竞争回顾在解释排行榜衡量了什么、隐藏评估如何改变结论以及哪些设计模式得到了奖励时非常有用。我们重新审视了CODS 2025 \assetopslive{}挑战赛，这是一个基于\assetops{}的隐私感知Codabench竞赛，针对工业多智能体编排。我们结合了最终排名表、包含300次提交的服务器日志、149个团队注册、最佳提交导出、组织者获胜者报告、伴随的\assetopslive{}系统论文以及经过验证的规划跟踪源代码树。五个结果突出。首先，公共规划排行榜饱和在72.73%，更丰富的提示并未提高该峰值。其次，隐藏评估改变了故事：公共分数和私有分数在规划中中等相关（r=0.69），但在执行中负相关（r=-0.13），几个公共执行系统得分为45.45%的团队在隐藏集上达到了63.64%。第三，\tmatch{}项在官方综合分数中数值上几乎惰性——在0-1尺度上与0-100百分比的分数结合，它在每个跟踪中最多贡献0.05分，重新缩放将交换前两名团队。第四，竞赛在操作上基于账户，但实质上基于团队：149个注册团队减少到24个有非零公共分数和11个完全排名，而52.3%的去重注册列出了多个用户名。第五，成功的执行方法大多改进了防护栏——响应选择、污染清理、回退和上下文控制——而不是新颖的智能体架构。这些发现识别了评估奖励了哪些行为，并激励了对规模感知的复合、技能水平诊断和版本化工件发布的需求。

Original abstract: Competition retrospectives are useful when they explain what a leaderboard measured, how hidden evaluation changed conclusions, and which design patterns were rewarded. We revisit the CODS 2025 \assetopslive{} challenge, a privacy-aware Codabench competition on industrial multi-agent orchestration built on \assetops{}. We combine final rank sheets, a 300-submission server log, 149-team registrations, best-submission exports, the organizer winners report, the companion \assetopslive{} system paper, and verified planning-track source trees. Five results stand out. First, the public planning leaderboard saturates at 72.73\%, and richer prompts do not improve that peak. Second, hidden evaluation changes the story: public and private scores correlate moderately in planning ($r{=}0.69$) but negatively in execution ($r{=}{-}0.13$), with several 45.45\% public execution systems reaching 63.64\% on the hidden set. Third, the \tmatch{} term is numerically almost inert in the official composite -- combined on a 0--1 scale with 0--100 percentage scores, it contributes at most 0.05 points per track, and rescaling would swap the top two teams. Fourth, the competition is operationally account-based but substantively team-based: 149 registered teams reduce to 24 with non-zero public scores and 11 fully ranked, while 52.3\% of deduplicated registrations list multiple usernames. Fifth, successful execution methods mostly improve guardrails -- response selection, contamination cleanup, fallback, and context control -- rather than novel agent architectures. These findings identify which behaviors the evaluation rewarded, and motivate scale-aware composites, skill-level diagnostics, and versioned artifact release.
