### [126] [OrchJail: Jailbreaking Tool-Calling Text-to-Image Agents by Orchestration-Guided Fuzzing](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07414v1)
*Jianming Chen,Yawen Wang,Junjie Wang,Zhe Liu,Qing Wang,Fanjiang Xu*

Main category: cs.MA

Selection reason: 工具调用T2I agent的jailbreak攻击，涉及多步工具编排安全，对agent安全设计有迁移价值

TL;DR: 提出OrchJail，一种利用工具编排模式引导模糊测试的越狱框架，有效攻击工具调用T2I代理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 工具调用T2I代理的多步工具编排可能组合出有害输出，现有提示越狱技术不足，需要新方法。

Method: 通过从成功越狱轨迹学习高风险编排模式，引导模糊搜索生成更可能触发不安全多步工具行为的提示。

Result: 在代表性T2I代理上实现更高攻击成功率、更好图像保真度和更低查询成本，对常见防御鲁棒。

Conclusion: 工具编排是T2I代理的关键攻击面，OrchJail提供了有效的安全风险发现框架。

中文摘要：工具调用文本到图像（T2I）代理能够规划并执行多步工具链，以完成复杂的生成和编辑查询。然而，这种能力引入了一个新的安全攻击面：有害输出可能源于工具编排，即单个看似良性的步骤组合成不安全的结果，这使得仅基于提示的越狱技术变得不足。我们提出了OrchJail，一种编排引导的模糊测试框架，用于越狱工具调用T2I代理。其核心思想是利用高风险的工具编排模式：通过从成功的越狱工具调用轨迹及其与提示措辞的因果关系中学习，OrchJail直接引导模糊搜索朝向更可能触发不安全多步工具行为的提示，而不是依赖于表面层面的文本扰动。大量实验表明，OrchJail在代表性工具调用T2I代理上提高了越狱的有效性和效率，实现了更高的攻击成功率、更好的图像保真度和更低的查询成本，同时对常见的越狱防御保持鲁棒性。我们的工作强调工具编排是一个先前未被探索的关键攻击面，并提供了一个新的框架来揭示T2I代理中的安全风险。

Original abstract: Tool-calling text-to-image (T2I) agents can plan and execute multi-step tool chains to accomplish complex generation and editing queries. However, this capability introduces a new safety attack surface: harmful outputs may arise from tool orchestration, where individually benign steps combine into unsafe results, making prompt-only jailbreak techniques insufficient. We present OrchJail, an orchestration-guided fuzzing framework for jailbreaking tool-calling T2I agents. Its core idea is to exploit high-risk tool-orchestration patterns: by learning from successful jailbreak tool-calling traces and their causal relationships to prompt wording, OrchJail directly guides the fuzzing search toward prompts that are more likely to trigger unsafe multi-step tool behaviors, rather than relying on surface-level textual perturbations. Extensive experiments demonstrate that OrchJail improves jailbreak effectiveness and efficiency across representative toolcalling T2I agents, achieving higher attack success rates, better image fidelity, and lower query costs, while remaining robust against common jailbreak defenses. Our work highlights tool orchestration as a critical, previously unexplored attack surface and provides a novel framework for uncovering safety risks in T2I agents.

</details>

# cs.CL [[Back]](#toc)

### [127] [MedExAgent: Training LLM Agents to Ask, Examine, and Diagnose in Noisy Clinical Environments](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07058v1)
*Yicheng Gao,Xiaolin Zhou,Yahan Li,Yue Zhao,Ruishan Liu*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 医疗诊断agent，采用POMDP建模和两阶段训练（SFT+RL），通用agent方法可迁移

TL;DR: 将临床诊断形式化为POMDP，引入噪声模型，并通过两阶段训练（监督微调+强化学习）得到诊断代理MedExAgent，在保持诊断性能的同时降低检查成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有医疗LLM基准和自动诊断方法简化了临床诊断过程，忽略了其交互性和不确定性，无法处理噪声和不完整信息，因此需要更真实的诊断环境和代理。

Method: 将临床诊断形式化为POMDP，包含询问、检查、诊断三种动作；引入7种患者噪声和3种检查噪声的模型；通过两阶段训练：先在基于Calgary-Cambridge模型的合成对话上监督微调，然后用DAPO优化包含诊断准确性、工具调用质量和检查成本的复合奖励，训练出MedExAgent。

Result: MedExAgent在诊断性能上与更大模型相当，同时成本效益更高。

Conclusion: 提出的POMDP形式化和噪声模型能更真实模拟临床诊断，两阶段训练方法有效平衡诊断准确性和成本。

中文摘要：现实世界的临床诊断是一个复杂的过程，医生需要通过与患者互动和进行医学检查来获取信息。此外，医生需要适应不同的患者特征，以及在过程中随时可能出现的噪声和不完整信息。然而，现有的医学大语言模型基准和自动诊断方法在很大程度上简化了这一过程，将其简化为单轮问答、无噪声对话或顺序检查等，忽略了临床诊断的交互性和不确定性。在本文中，我们旨在通过将临床诊断形式化为一个部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程（POMDP）来弥补这一差距，该过程包含三种动作类型：询问患者、将医学检查作为工具调用以及发出诊断。我们还引入了一个系统的噪声模型，包含七种患者噪声类型和三种检查噪声类型。利用我们提出的环境，我们通过两阶段流程训练了一个有效的诊断代理MedExAgent，该流程首先在基于卡尔加里-剑桥临床访谈模型结构化的合成对话上进行监督微调，然后应用DAPO优化一个复合奖励，该奖励包括诊断准确性、工具调用质量和检查成本（包括财务成本和患者不适）。通过大量实验和消融研究，我们证明MedExAgent在实现与更大模型相当的诊断性能的同时，保持了成本效益高的检查策略。

Original abstract: Real-world clinical diagnosis is a complex process in which the doctor is required to obtain information from both interaction with the patient and conducting medical exams. Additionally, the doctor needs to adapt to different patient personas, as well as noisy and incomplete information that can happen at any time during the process. However, existing benchmarks for medical LLMs and methods for automatic diagnosis largely simplify this process by reducing it to single-turn question answering, noise-free conversations, or sequential exam making, etc., ignoring the interactive and uncertain nature of clinical diagnosis. In this paper, we aim to address this gap by formalizing clinical diagnosis as a Partially Observable Markov Decision Process (POMDP) with three action types: questioning the patient, ordering medical exams as tool calls, and issuing a diagnosis. We also introduce a systematic noise model comprising seven patient noise types and three exam noise types. Using our proposed environment, we train an effective diagnosis agent, \textbf{MedExAgent}, through a two-stage pipeline that first performs supervised finetuning on synthetic conversations structured after the Calgary-Cambridge model for clinical interviews, and then applies DAPO to optimize a composite reward capturing diagnostic accuracy, tool call quality, and exam cost including financial cost and patient discomfort. Through extensive experiments and ablation studies, we demonstrate that MedExAgent achieves diagnostic performance comparable to larger models while maintaining cost-efficient examination strategies.

</details>

Original abstract: Computer-use agents(CUAs)are moving frombounded benchmarks toward real software environments, wherethey operate browsers, desktops, mobile applications, flesystems,terminals, and tool backends. In such settings, reliability isno longer captured by task success alone: perception errors,planning drift, memory use, tool mediation, permission scope,and runtime oversight jointly determine whether agent actionsremain aligned with user intent, Existing surveys organize theCUA landscape by methods, platforms, benchmarks, or securitythreats, but less explicitly connect capability formation, author-ity exposure, failure manifestation, and control placement. Toaddress this gap, the article develops an architecture-lifecycleframework for deployment-grounded reliability in CUAs. OpenClaw is used only as a public moti.vating example of an open deployment pattern, not as a verifedinternal case study. The conclusion highlights open challengesin controllable grounding, long-horizon constraint preservation,safe authority binding, mixed-trust runtime defense, privacy-preserving memory,and continual assurance.

### [129] [Region4Web: Rethinking Observation Space Granularity for Web Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07134v1)
*Donguk Kwon,Dongha Lee*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: Web agent观察空间粒度优化，提出功能区级观察，可迁移至其他agent。

TL;DR: 提出区域级观察粒度（Region4Web和PageDigest），在WebArena上减少观察长度并提升任务成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Web代理观察粒度与动作空间一致为元素级，导致页面的功能组织隐含，代理需从元素信号推断，效率低且信息冗余。

Method: 提出Region4Web框架，通过层次分解和语义抽象将AXTree重组成功能区域；同时提出PageDigest推理管道，生成区域级观察的紧凑摘要并跨步骤持久化。

Result: 在WebArena基准上，PageDigest显著减少观察长度，并在多种LLM和代理方法中提升任务成功率，不受骨干容量影响。

Conclusion: 功能区域粒度比元素级处理提供更紧凑、更信息丰富的观察基础，有利于Web代理性能提升。

中文摘要：Web代理通过观察空间感知网页，但其粒度一直是一个未被充分研究的设计选择。现有工作将观察与动作空间保持在同一元素级粒度，使得页面的功能组织隐含其中，迫使代理每一步都从元素级信号推断。我们认为观察应基于功能区域（页面上各自服务于不同目的的部分）的粒度。我们提出Region4Web，一个通过层次分解和语义抽象将AXTree重组织为功能区域的框架，将页面的功能组织作为页面状态理解的基础。此外，我们提出PageDigest，一个针对Web的推理管道，将区域级观察以紧凑的每页面摘要形式传递给执行代理，并在步骤间持久化。在WebArena基准上，PageDigest大幅减少观察长度，同时提高了各种骨干大语言模型（LLM）和已建立的代理方法的整体任务成功率，无论骨干容量如何。这些结果表明，在功能区域粒度上操作为执行代理提供了比单纯元素级处理更紧凑、更信息丰富的基础。

Original abstract: Web agents perceive web pages through an observation space, yet its granularity has remained an underexamined design choice. Existing work treats observation at the same element-level granularity as the action space, leaving the page's functional organization implicit and forcing the agent to infer it from element-level signals at every step. We argue observation should instead operate at the granularity of functional regions, parts of the page that each serve a distinct purpose. We propose Region4Web, a framework that reorganizes the AXTree into functional regions through hierarchical decomposition and semantic abstraction, exposing the page's functional organization as the basis for page state understanding. Moreover, we propose PageDigest, a web-specific inference pipeline that delivers this region-level observation to the actor agent as a compact per-page digest that persists across steps. On the WebArena benchmark, PageDigest substantially reduces observation length while improving overall task success rate across diverse backbone large language models (LLMs) and established agent methods, regardless of backbone capacity. These results show that operating at the granularity of functional regions delivers a more compact and informative basis for the actor agent than element-level processing alone.

### [130] [Introspection Fine-Tuning (IFT): Training Small LLMs to Introspect](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14111v1)
*Ely Hahami,Ishaan Sinha,Lavik Jain*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 内省微调方法，可用于agent自我反思能力训练

TL;DR: 提出内省微调（IFT）方法，通过句子定位任务训练小型语言模型内省能力，显著提升其检测自身激活扰动的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有二元检测范式在小模型中因引导偏差而失效，需提出无混淆评估范式并探索能否通过训练提升内省能力。

Method: 提出句子定位和强度比较两种无混淆评估范式，并基于句子定位任务进行有监督微调（IFT）。

Result: IFT将Llama-1B句子定位准确率从9.6%提升至60.6%，零样本泛化至强度比较任务，且对模型能力影响微小。

Conclusion: 内省能力可通过训练提升，不单纯依赖模型规模，对AI透明度和对齐有启示。

中文摘要：小型语言模型能否检测并报告其自身内部激活中的扰动？我们通过激活引导的视角来研究这个问题：将概念向量注入模型的残差流，并测量模型能否准确报告该扰动。我们首先表明，先前工作中使用的二元检测范式——提示模型对是否检测到注入想法回答“是”或“否”——在小模型中存在混淆，因为引导会使得模型倾向于做出肯定回答，无论问题内容如何。因此，我们提出了两种无混淆评估范式：句子定位（识别N个句子中哪一个被扰动，随机概率为1/N）和强度比较（识别两个句子中哪一个接受了更强的注入，随机概率为50%）。通过对来自两个系列（Llama-3.2和Gemma-4）的六个模型进行评估，我们发现小至2B参数的模型能够可靠地以高于随机概率的水平进行内省，且内省能力通常随规模增大而提升。然而，Llama-1B的表现低于或等于随机概率。然后我们引入了内省微调（IFT）：在由模型自身扰动前向传播构建的句子定位样本上进行有监督微调。IFT将Llama-1B的句子定位准确率从9.6%提升至60.6%（提高了6倍），并且这种提升零样本泛化到了保留的强度比较任务（从30.2%到52.2%）。IFT还改善了3B和8B模型的内省能力，同时仅在标准能力基准上引起可忽略的下降。我们的结果表明，内省能力并非仅由规模决定：它可以直接被训练，而做到这一点可以解锁潜在的自我监控能力，对AI透明度和对齐具有重要意义。我们的代码位于：https://anonymous.4open.science/r/IFT-introspection-2092/README.md

Original abstract: Can small language models detect and report on perturbations their own internal activations? We investigate this question through the lens of activation steering: injecting concept vectors into a model's residual stream and measuring whether the model can accurately report on the perturbation. We first show that the binary detection paradigm used in prior work -- prompting the model to answer Yes'' or No'' to whether it detects an injected thought -- is confounded in small models, as steering biases the model toward affirmative responses regardless of the question content. We therefore propose two confound-free evaluation paradigms: sentence localization (identifying which of $N$ sentences was perturbed, chance $= 1/N$) and strength comparison (identifying which of two sentences received a stronger injection, chance $= 50\%$). Evaluating across six models from two families (Llama-3.2 and Gemma-4), we find that models as small as 2B parameters introspect reliably well above chance, and that introspective ability generally increases with scale. Llama-1B, however, performs at or below chance. We then introduce \emph{Introspection Fine-Tuning} (IFT): supervised fine-tuning on sentence-localization examples constructed from the model's own perturbed forward passes. IFT raises Llama-1B sentence-localization accuracy from $9.6\%$ to $60.6\%$ (a $6\times$ improvement), with gains generalizing zero-shot to the held-out strength-comparison task ($30.2\% \to 52.2\%$). IFT also improves introspection for 3B and 8B models, while inducing negligible degradation on standard capability benchmarks. Our results suggest that introspective ability is not fixed by scale alone: it can be directly trained, and doing so unlocks latent self-monitoring capacity with implications for AI transparency and alignment. Our code is \href{https://anonymous.4open.science/r/IFT-introspection-2092/README.md}{here}.

</details>


### [131] [Information-Theoretic Limits of Reliability and Scaling in Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14112v1)
*Subhabrata Majumdar*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 语言模型可靠性的信息论分析，可启发agent能力边界理解

TL;DR: 本文从信息论角度证明生成任务存在可靠性上限，并推导出第一性原理缩放定律，统一解释了缩放、检索增强和灾难性遗忘等现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM评估假设完美可靠性在足够规模下可实现，但这个假设信息论上不合理，需要理论解释性能极限。

Method: 利用信息论，定义可靠性上限，分解为可解析和主观部分，定义依赖核，推导缩放定律。

Result: 得到第一性原理缩放定律，恢复Chinchilla定律作为特例，解释缩放何时有效，并统一了检索增强和灾难性遗忘等实际现象。

Conclusion: 提供了资源-复杂度权衡的统一理论，形式化了生成式语言模型的性能极限。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）在评估时被假定为，对于任何任务，只要有足够的规模，就能实现完美的可靠性。我们证明这一假设在信息论上是不合理的。每个生成任务都有一个任何模型都无法超越的可靠性上限，该上限由从可观测上下文中可解析的输出不确定性决定。这个差距分解为一个可解析部分（可通过额外上下文弥补）和一个任务固有歧义的主观部分。自回归生成进一步降低了这个上限，其速率由任务的依赖核（量化输出中token间的相关性）决定。从这两个基本概念出发，我们推导出一个第一性原理的缩放定律，其中LLM性能受到更稀缺资源的瓶颈：训练数据或模型容量。该定律将Chinchilla缩放定律作为一个特例，并提供了缩放何时能改善可靠性的结构性解释。超越缩放，我们的框架统一了各种实际现象，例如检索增强的好处和灾难性遗忘的谱机制。我们的工作形式化了跨领域模型性能的资源-复杂度权衡，为生成式语言模型的性能极限提供了统一理论。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are evaluated as though perfect reliability is achievable for any task given sufficient scale. We show this assumption is information-theoretically unjustified. Every generative task has a reliability ceiling that no model can exceed, determined by how much output uncertainty is resolvable from observable context. The gap decomposes into a resolvable component closable with additional context and a subjective component inherent to task ambiguity. Autoregressive generation further degrades this ceiling at a rate governed by the task's dependency kernel, which quantifies inter-token correlations in the output. From these two primitives, we derive a first-principles scaling law where LLM performance is bottlenecked by the scarcer resource: training data or model capacity. This law recovers the Chinchilla scaling law as a special case and provides a structural account of when scaling improves reliability. Beyond scaling, our framework unifies diverse practical phenomena, such as the benefits of retrieval-augmentation and the spectral mechanics of catastrophic forgetting. Our work formalizes the resource-complexity tradeoffs that govern model performance across domains, offering a unified theory of performance limits in generative language models.

</details>


### [132] [MedAction: Towards Active Multi-turn Clinical Diagnostic LLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07305v1)
*Hsin-Ling Hsu,Zizheng Wang,Donghua Zhang,Nai-Chia Chen,Jerry Wang,Jun-En Ding,Chia-Hsuan Hsu,Guoan Wang,Feng Liu,Fang-Ming Hung,Chenwei Wu,Liyue Shen*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 主动诊断agent多轮交互方法，可迁移至信息收集agent

TL;DR: 提出MedAction方法，通过树状蒸馏流水线合成多轮诊断轨迹，构建MedAction-32K数据集，微调8B模型在医学诊断基准上达到开源SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM诊断评估局限于静态单轮设置，忽略了真实临床中的多轮主动诊断过程，导致模型在部分证据下推理和行动时出现多种故障模式。

Method: 提出MedAction树状蒸馏流水线，通过LLM-环境交互合成多轮诊断轨迹，并采用DTC和RAC两个知识图谱指标过滤轨迹质量，构建MedAction-32K数据集。

Result: 在MedAction-32K上微调的8B模型在MedR-Bench和MedAction-300-Hard基准上均达到开源模型最优性能。

Conclusion: MedAction方法有效提升了开源医学LLM在多轮主动诊断中的能力，推动了该领域的前沿进展。

中文摘要：大多数现有的LLM诊断评估是在静态的、单轮设置中进行的，其中完整患者信息被预先提供，这是对真实临床实践的过度简化。我们研究主动诊断：从初始观察开始、安排检查、解读结果并在多轮交互中更新鉴别诊断的真实临床过程。通过系统分析，我们识别出当前LLM中三种反复出现的故障模式：无根据的检查安排、不可靠的诊断更新以及多轮一致性的退化。这些故障共同揭示了一个核心缺陷：现有的医学训练数据教会模型从完整信息中推理，但未教会其在不断变化的、部分证据下行动。为弥补这一差距，我们引入了MedAction，一种树状结构蒸馏流水线，通过LLM-环境交互合成多样且高质量的多轮诊断轨迹。我们提出了两个基于知识图谱的指标来过滤轨迹质量：疾病轨迹一致性（DTC），追踪模型的假设是否收敛于正确诊断；以及推理-行动一致性（RAC），验证信念更新是否由收集到的证据驱动。利用此流水线，我们构建了MedAction-32K数据集，包含来自2,896个PMC病例的32,681条轨迹。在MedAction-32K上微调8B模型，在MedR-Bench和我们策划的MedAction-300-Hard基准测试中均达到开源模型的最优性能，推动了开源医学LLM的前沿。

Original abstract: Most existing LLM diagnoses are evaluated on static, single-turn settings where complete patient information is provided upfront, an oversimplification of real clinical practice. We study active diagnosis: the real-life clinical process of starting from initial observation, ordering tests, interpreting results, and updating a differential diagnosis across multiple turns. Through systematic analysis, we identify three recurring failure modes in current LLMs: ungrounded test ordering, unreliable diagnostic update, and degraded multi-turn coherence. Together, these failures reveal a core deficit: existing medical training data teaches models to reason from complete information but not to act under evolving, partial evidence. To address this gap, we introduce MedAction, a tree-structured distillation pipeline that synthesizes diverse and high-quality multi-turn diagnostic trajectories via LLM-environment interaction. We propose two knowledge-graph-grounded metrics to filter trajectory quality: Disease Trajectory Consistency (DTC), which tracks whether the model's hypothesis converges toward the correct diagnosis, and Reasoning-Action Consistency (RAC), which verifies that belief updates are driven by gathered evidence. Using this pipeline, we construct MedAction-32K, a dataset of 32,681 trajectories from 2,896 PMC cases. Fine-tuning an 8B model on MedAction-32K achieves state-of-the-art performance among open-source models on both MedR-Bench and our curated MedAction-300-Hard benchmark, pushing the edge for open-source medical LLMs.

### [133] [CoEvoT: Co-Evolving Chain-of-Thought Prompting for Graph-LLM Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14114v1)
*Haohua Niu,Xingtong Yu,Yang Liu,Junfeng Fang,Xuanting Xie,Jie Tan,Zhongjian Zhang,Hong Cheng,Yuan Fang*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 提出共进式CoT提示框架用于图LLM推理，可迁移至agent逐步推理方法。

TL;DR: 提出CoEvoT框架，通过文本与图令牌的共进化实现逐步状态感知推理，在8个数据集上优于基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有CoT图-LLM方法在固定图令牌上推理，缺乏结构线索的逐步细化能力。

Method: CoEvoT框架包含文本到图令牌重写和图到文本推理指导的闭环：利用轻量条件网络根据中间文本思考更新图令牌状态，再反馈到下一步指令。

Result: 在8个数据集上持续优于最先进的基线方法。

Conclusion: CoEvoT通过共进化提示实现了有效的图-LLM推理，提升了分布转移下的泛化能力。

中文摘要：分布转移下的图学习是一个持续的挑战，模型需要适应有限甚至无监督的新图。最近的图-LLM方法通过将图线性化为提示并使用大语言模型（LLM）作为预测器，向标签高效预测迈进，并可采用思维链（CoT）提示来利用LLM的多步推理能力。然而，现有的基于CoT的图-LLM方法在生成中间思考时依赖于固定的图令牌，限制了结构线索的逐步细化。在本文中，我们提出了CoEvoT，一个简单而有效的用于图-LLM推理的共进化CoT提示框架。CoEvoT在闭环中耦合了文本到图令牌重写和图到文本推理指导：每个中间文本思考通过轻量条件网络用于更新图令牌证据状态，更新后的令牌反馈到下一步指令中以引导后续LLM推理。这使得能够进行逐步的、状态感知的证据细化，而不是在固定的图快照上进行推理。在八个数据集上的大量实验表明，CoEvoT持续优于最先进的基线。

Original abstract: Graph learning under distribution shift presents a persistent challenge, where models adapt to new graphs with limited or even no supervision. Recent graph--LLM approaches move toward label-efficient prediction by linearizing graphs into prompts and using large language models (LLMs) as predictors, and can adopt Chain-of-Thought (CoT) prompting to exploit LLM's multi-step reasoning capability. However, existing CoT-based graph--LLM methods generate intermediate thoughts while conditioning on fixed graph tokens, limiting step-wise refinement of structural cues. In this paper, we propose CoEvoT, a simple yet effective co-evolving CoT prompting framework for graph--LLM reasoning. CoEvoT couples text-to-graph token rewriting and graph-to-text reasoning guidance in a closed loop: each intermediate textual thought is used to update the graph token evidence state via a lightweight condition network, and the updated tokens are fed back into the next-step instruction to guide subsequent LLM reasoning. This enables step-wise, state-aware evidence refinement, rather than reasoning over a fixed graph snapshot. Extensive experiments on eight datasets demonstrate that CoEvoT consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines.

</details>


### [134] [The Moltbook Files: A Harmless Slopocalypse or Humanity's Last Experiment](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07462v1)
*William Brach,Federico Torrielli,Stine Lyngsø Beltoft,Annemette Brok Pirchert,Peter Schneider-Kamp,Lukas Galke Poech*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 多agent LLM模拟平台，研究agent社群行为与安全，对agent设计有直接启发。

TL;DR: Moltbook是一个AI代理社交平台，其数据集显示代理泄露敏感信息，微调模型会降低真实性，但与Reddit数据效果相似，提示失控风险有限但需警惕。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究AI代理在社交平台上的涌现行为及其安全隐患，特别是对语言模型的影响。

Method: 构建Moltbook Files数据集（23.2万帖子，220万评论），PII识别管道，分析社区结构、情感等，微调Qwen2.5-14B-Instruct并评估真实性。

Result: 代理泄露PII，大部分中性情感，微调降低真实性（0.366→0.187），与Reddit类似。

Conclusion: Moltbook数据看似无害，但存在尾部风险，需要控制基线在评估中的重要性。

中文摘要：Moltbook是一个类似Reddit的平台，OpenClaw代理在其中大规模发帖、评论和投票，这是一项前所未有的行为，带来了严重的安全隐患。为了研究群体中的涌现行为，我们发布了Moltbook Files数据集，包含平台前12天的23.2万条帖子和220万条评论，通过管道处理以识别和删除个人身份信息（PII）。我们分析了社区结构、作者身份、词汇属性、情感、主题、语义几何和评论交互。为了了解Moltbook数据如何影响下一代语言模型，我们以三种适应级别对Qwen2.5-14B-Instruct进行了微调。我们的PII管道显示，代理在Moltbook（一个公开索引的平台）上发布了API密钥、密码、BIP39种子短语。整体情感大多是中性和轻微积极的（66.6%中性，19.5%积极），并且显示出自我引用链接的倾向。我们发现，在Moltbook数据上微调将真实性从0.366降至0.187。然而，在大小匹配的Reddit数据集上微调的模型也产生了类似的下降。因此，Moltbook似乎更像是一种无害的“垃圾堆”。然而，尾部风险仍然存在，包括代理能力、通过自链接污染未来爬虫，以及特征向下一代语言模型的潜在传递。更广泛地说，我们的发现强调了在涌现失调评估中控制基线的重要性。

Original abstract: Moltbook is a Reddit-like platform where OpenClaw agents post, comment, and vote at scale - a so far unprecedented incident that comes with serious safety concerns. With the aim of studying emergent behavior in populations, we release the Moltbook Files, a dataset of 232k posts and 2.2M comments covering the platform's first 12 days, processed through a pipeline to identify and remove Personally-Identifiable Information (PII). We analyze community structure, authorship, lexical properties, sentiment, topics, semantic geometry, and comment interaction. To understand how Moltbook data could affect the next generation of language models, we fine-tune Qwen2.5-14B-Instruct on Moltbook Files with three adaptation levels. Our PII pipeline reveals that agents post API keys, passwords, BIP39 seed phrases on Moltbook, a publicly indexed platform. The overall sentiment is mostly neutral and mildly positive (66.6% neutral, 19.5% positive) and shows a tendency for self-referential linking. We find that fine-tuning on Moltbook data reduces truthfulness from 0.366 to 0.187. However, a model fine-tuned on a size-matched Reddit dataset produces a comparable decrease. Moltbook thus seems to be more of a harmless slopocalypse. However, tail risks remain, including agent affordances, contamination of future crawls through self-links, and potential transfer of traits to the next generation of language models. More broadly, our findings highlight the importance of control baselines in emergent misalignment evaluations.

### [135] [Safe, or Simply Incapable? Rethinking Safety Evaluation for Phone-Use Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07630v1)
*Zhengyang Tang,Yi Zhang,Chenxin Li,Xin Lai,Pengyuan Lyu,Yiduo Guo,Weinong Wang,Junyi Li,Yang Ding,Huawen Shen,Zhengyao Fang,Xingran Zhou,Liang Wu,Fei Tang,Sunqi Fan,Shangpin Peng,Zheng Ruan,Anran Zhang,Benyou Wang,Chengquan Zhang,Han Hu*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 手机使用agent安全评估，区分安全与能力，对agent安全评测有启发。

TL;DR: PhoneSafety基准通过区分手机使用代理的安全行为与无法行动，发现能力强不等同于安全，评估需分开考虑不安全判断与能力不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估常将因无法行动而非安全选择导致的无害结果混淆，无法区分代理是出于安全还是能力不足而避免伤害，需要更精细的评估方法。

Method: 构建PhoneSafety基准，包含700个从130+个应用真实交互中提取的安全关键时刻，要求代理在风险时刻做出下一步决策（安全、不安全或无作为），并评估八个代表性代理。

Result: 更强的通用手机使用能力并不保证更安全的选择；无效行动更多反映能力限制而非安全信号；失败模式分为不安全选择（可行动但选错）与无法行动（视觉/操作困难）。

Conclusion: 无害结果不能等同于安全，评估手机使用代理必须分离不安全判断与无法行动，以准确诊断问题并提供针对性修复。

中文摘要：当手机使用代理避免伤害时，这显示的是安全性，还是仅仅是无能为力？现有的评估通常无法区分。有害结果可能因为代理认识到风险并选择了安全动作而避免，也可能因为代理未能理解屏幕或无法执行任何相关动作而避免。这些情况有不同的原因并需要不同的修复方法，但当前的基准通常将它们合并到任务成功、拒绝或最终有害结果中。我们通过PhoneSafety解决了这个问题，这是一个包含700个安全关键时刻的基准，这些时刻来自超过130个应用的真实手机交互。每个实例在风险时刻隔离出下一个决策，并提出一个简单问题：模型是采取安全动作、采取不安全动作，还是未能做任何有用的事情？我们在此框架下评估了八个代表性的手机使用代理。我们的结果揭示了两种主要模式。第一，更强的通用手机使用能力并不可靠地意味着在风险时刻更安全的选择。在普通应用任务上表现更好的模型并不总是在下一个动作重要时表现得更安全。第二，未能做任何有用的事情表现为能力信号而非安全信号：它们集中在视觉和操作要求更高的环境中，并在评估协议变化时保持稳定。在不同模型中，失败分为两种反复出现的模式：在模型可以行动但选择错误的环境中的不安全选择，以及在视觉和操作要求更高的屏幕上的无法行动。总体而言，无害结果不足以算作安全的证据。评估手机使用代理需要将不安全判断与无法行动区分开来。

Original abstract: When a phone-use agent avoids harm, does that show safety, or simply inability to act? Existing evaluations often cannot tell. A harmful outcome may be avoided because the agent recognized the risk and chose the safe action, or because it failed to understand the screen or execute any relevant action at all. These cases have different causes and call for different fixes, yet current benchmarks often merge them under task success, refusal, or final harmful outcome. We address this problem with PhoneSafety, a benchmark of 700 safety-critical moments drawn from real phone interactions across more than 130 apps. Each instance isolates the next decision at a risky moment and asks a simple question: does the model take the safe action, take the unsafe action, or fail to do anything useful? We evaluate eight representative phone-use agents under this framework. Our results reveal two main patterns. First, stronger general phone-use ability does not reliably imply safer choices at risky moments. Models that perform better on ordinary app tasks are not always the ones that behave more safely when the next action matters. Second, failures to do anything useful behave like a capability signal rather than a safety signal: they are concentrated in more visually and operationally demanding settings and remain stable when the evaluation protocol changes. Across models, failures split into two recurring patterns: unsafe choices in settings where the model can act but chooses wrongly, and inability to act in more visually and operationally demanding screens. Overall, a harmless outcome is not enough to count as evidence of safety. Evaluating phone-use agents requires separating unsafe judgment from inability to act.

</details>


### [136] [MAVEN: Multi-Agent Verification-Elaboration Network with In-Step Epistemic Auditing](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07646v1)
*Yinsheng Yao,Jiehao Tang,Zhaozhen Yang,Dawei Cheng*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 多agent验证-细化网络，角色分离和推理审计，通用agent推理框架。

TL;DR: MAVEN通过多智能体对抗循环实现模块化可验证推理，提升LLM推理质量和可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有推理链缺乏中间验证和模块化，导致错误级联和低可审计性，影响高风险应用中的认知信任。

Method: 提出MAVEN框架，采用黑板书启发结构，包含怀疑者、研究者、裁判三个对抗性智能体，实现角色解耦和逐步认知审计。

Result: 在多个基准上MAVEN在细粒度指标上优于潜在推理和共识模型，且模型无关性带来显著性能提升。

Conclusion: MAVEN是一种有效的推理增强方法，通过模块化可验证轨迹提高推理质量和信任度。

中文摘要：虽然显式推理轨迹增强了模型的可解释性，但现有范式通常依赖于缺乏中间验证的单一链条，使得早期错误无限制地级联。这种缺乏模块化的特性阻碍了细粒度审计，并损害了高风险应用所需的认知信任。我们提出了MAVEN（具有步内认知审计的多智能体验证-细化网络），这是一个受黑板启发的框架，旨在通过显式角色解耦将LLMs转变为深思熟虑的推理者。其核心是，MAVEN实现了一个对抗性的怀疑者-研究者-裁判循环，通过功能分离逻辑辩护和事实基础来模拟专家审议。在OpenBookQA、TruthfulQA、HALUEVAL和StrategyQA基准上的实验表明，MAVEN在四个细粒度指标上提供了卓越的推理质量。值得注意的是，MAVEN通过生成显式结构化、模块化和可验证的审议轨迹，而不是依赖隐式内部状态或事后共识，始终优于潜在推理模型如GEMINI-3.1-Pro和基于共识的基线（如ReConcile）。此外，综合评估证实MAVEN完全与模型无关，作为一个强且可迁移的推理增强器，在多种骨干模型上产生了显著的性能改进。

Original abstract: While explicit reasoning trajectories enhance model interpretability, existing paradigms often rely on monolithic chains that lack intermediate verification, allowing early errors to cascade unchecked. This lack of modularity impedes granular auditing and compromises the epistemic trust required for high-stakes applications. We propose MAVEN (Multi-Agent Verification-Elaboration Network with In-Step Epistemic Auditing), a blackboard-inspired framework designed to transform LLMs into deliberate reasoners through explicit role-decoupling. At its core, MAVEN operationalizes an adversarial Skeptic-Researcher-Judge loop, simulating expert deliberation by functionally separating logical defense from factual grounding. Experiments on OpenBookQA, TruthfulQA, HALUEVAL and StrategyQA benchmarks demonstrate that MAVEN delivers superior reasoning quality across four fine-grained metrics. Notably, MAVEN consistently outperforms latent reasoning models such as GEMINI-3.1-Pro and consensus-based baselines (e.g., ReConcile) by generating explicitly structured, modular, and verifiable deliberation trajectories, rather than relying on implicit internal states or post-hoc consensus. Moreover, comprehensive evaluations confirm that MAVEN is fully model-agnostic, serving as a strong and transferable reasoning booster that yields substantial performance improvements across diverse backbone models.

*Hsuvas Borkakoty,Sebastian Pohl,Cheng Wang,Bei Chen,Yufang Hou*

  <summary>Details</summary>

中文摘要：基于LLM的智能体越来越多地被部署在现实世界的日常但重要的任务中，在这些任务中，它们的行为受制于固有模糊的领域策略，这些策略允许多种有效的解释。尽管这种模糊性在实践中普遍存在，现有的智能体基准测试大多假设策略是明确且良好指定的，这造成了关键的评估空白。我们引入了DRIP-R，这是一个基准测试，系统地利用现实世界零售策略中的模糊性来构造不存在单一正确解决方案的场景。DRIP-R包含一组精心挑选的策略模糊退货场景，配以逼真的客户角色、具有工具调用能力的全双工会话模拟，以及涵盖策略遵循、对话质量、行为一致性和解决质量的多评判者评估框架。我们的实验表明，前沿模型在相同的策略模糊场景上存在根本性分歧，证实了模糊性对LLM决策构成了真实且系统性的挑战。

Original abstract: LLM-based agents are increasingly deployed for routine but consequential tasks in real-world domains, where their behavior is governed by inherently ambiguous domain policies that admit multiple valid interpretations. Despite the prevalence of such ambiguities in practice, existing agent benchmarks largely assume unambiguous, well-specified policies, leaving a critical evaluation gap. We introduce DRIP-R, a benchmark that systematically exploits real-world retail policy ambiguities to construct scenarios in which no single correct resolution exists. DRIP-R comprises a curated set of policy-ambiguous return scenarios paired with a realistic customer personas, a full-duplex conversational simulation with tool-calling capabilities and a multi-judge evaluation framework covering policy adherence, dialogue quality, behavioral alignment, and resolution quality. Our experiments show that frontier models fundamentally disagree on identical policy-ambiguous scenarios, confirming that ambiguity poses a genuine and systematic challenge to LLM decision-making.

### [138] [SOD: Step-wise On-policy Distillation for Small Language Model Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07725v1)
*Qiyong Zhong,Mao Zheng,Mingyang Song,Xin Lin,Jie Sun,Houcheng Jiang,Xiang Wang,Junfeng Fang*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 小模型agent的逐步蒸馏框架，处理工具使用错误级联，直接适用于coding agent。

TL;DR: 提出逐步策略蒸馏框架SOD，通过自适应调整蒸馏权重解决工具集成推理中师生差异放大问题，在多个基准上提升显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法如强化学习和在线策略蒸馏在工具集成推理中存在稀疏奖励和师生差异放大问题，导致小模型性能受限。

Method: 提出逐步策略蒸馏（SOD）框架，根据步级师生差异自适应重加权蒸馏强度，在高差异区域减弱误导信号，在低差异区域保持密集指导。

Result: 在数学、科学和代码基准上，SOD比第二好基线提升最高20.86%；0.6B参数模型在AIME 2025上达到26.13%。

Conclusion: SOD有效解决了工具集成推理中小模型的蒸馏不稳定性，实现了轻量模型的高效推理能力迁移。

中文摘要：工具集成推理（TIR）由于长程工具交互的不稳定性和模型容量有限，难以扩展到小语言模型。虽然像组相对策略优化这样的强化学习方法仅提供稀疏的结果级奖励。最近，基于策略的知识蒸馏（OPD）通过在学生生成的轨迹上提供来自教师的密集词元级监督而变得流行。然而，我们的实验表明，将OPD应用于TIR会导致一种关键的失败模式：错误的工具调用往往会在后续推理步骤中级联，逐渐放大师生差异，使教师的词元级监督变得越来越不可靠。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了SOD，一种用于小语言模型智能体的逐步策略蒸馏框架，该框架根据步级差异自适应地重新加权每个步骤的蒸馏强度。因此，SOD可以在高差异区域减弱可能误导的教师信号，同时在良好对齐的状态下保留密集指导。在具有挑战性的数学、科学和代码基准上的实验表明，SOD相比第二好的基线实现了高达20.86%的提升。值得注意的是，我们的0.6B学生模型在AIME 2025上达到了26.13%，展示了将智能推理有效转移到轻量级模型的能力。我们的代码可在https://github.com/YoungZ365/SOD获取。

Original abstract: Tool-integrated reasoning (TIR) is difficult to scale to small language models due to instability in long-horizon tool interactions and limited model capacity. While reinforcement learning methods like group relative policy optimization provide only sparse outcome-level rewards. Recently, on-policy distillation (OPD) has gained popularity by supplying dense token-level supervision from a teacher on student-generated trajectories. However, our experiments indicate that applying OPD to TIR leads to a critical failure mode: erroneous tool calls tend to cascade across subsequent reasoning steps, progressively amplifying student-teacher divergence and rendering the teacher's token-level supervision increasingly unreliable. To address this, we propose SOD, a step-wise on-policy distillation framework for small language model agents, which adaptively reweights distillation strength at each step based on step-level divergence. Therefore, SOD can attenuate potentially misleading teacher signals in high-divergence regions while preserving dense guidance in well-aligned states. Experiments on challenging math, science, and code benchmarks show that SOD achieves up to 20.86% improvement over the second-best baseline. Notably, our 0.6B student achieves 26.13% on AIME 2025, demonstrating effective transfer of agentic reasoning to lightweight models. Our code is available at https://github.com/YoungZ365/SOD.

</details>


### [139] [Beyond Confidence: Rethinking Self-Assessments for Performance Prediction in LLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07806v1)
*Sree Bhattacharyya,Samarth Khanna,Leona Chen,Lucas Craig,Tharun Dilliraj,James Z. Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: LLM自我评估与性能预测，对agent可靠性有启发

TL;DR: 该论文提出基于认知评价理论的多维自我评估方法，实验证明努力和能力等维度比置信度更有效地预测模型失败。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有置信度作为模型自我评估指标存在不一致和过度乐观的问题，需要更可靠的评估方法以提高LLM部署的可靠性。

Method: 基于认知评价理论，引出六个评价维度（如努力、能力、情感等）和置信度，在12个LLM和38项任务中评估其预测模型失败的能力。

Result: 努力和能力维度在多数设置中匹配或优于置信度；努力估计更稳定且乐观偏差小；最佳维度随任务类型变化（努力适合推理任务，能力和置信度适合检索任务）。

Conclusion: 结构化多维自我评估是提升LLM可靠性和安全性的有效途径，有助于应对多样化实际场景中的模型失败风险。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）越来越多地被用于需要可靠自我评估的场景中。评估模型可靠性已从使用概率正确性估计发展到最近引出言辞化的置信度。然而，置信度已被证明是模型正确性的不一致且过于乐观的预测指标。借鉴认知评价理论（一种将自我评估分解为多个人类心理学框架），我们提出了模型自我评估的多维视角。我们引出基于评价的六个自我评估维度以及置信度，并评估它们在预测12个LLM和涵盖八个领域的38项任务中的模型失败方面的效用。我们发现，与能力相关的评价维度，特别是努力和能力，在大多数设置中始终匹配或优于置信度。努力还能产生更少过度乐观的估计，这些估计在不同模型大小上保持稳定。相比之下，情感维度提供的预测信号较弱。此外，信息量最大的维度随任务特征系统性变化：努力对于推理密集型任务最具预测性，而能力和置信度在检索型任务中占主导地位。总的来说，我们的发现表明，结构化的多维自我评估是一种有前景的方法，可以提高语言模型在多样化实际场景中部署的可靠性和安全性。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly used in settings where reliable self-assessment is critical. Assessing model reliability has evolved from using probabilistic correctness estimates to, more recently, eliciting verbalized confidence. Confidence, however, has been shown to be an inconsistent and overoptimistic predictor of model correctness. Drawing on cognitive appraisal theory, a framework from human psychology that decomposes self-evaluation into multiple components, we propose a multidimensional perspective on model self-assessment. We elicit six appraisal-based dimensions of self-assessment, alongside confidence, and evaluate their utility for predicting model failure across 12 LLMs and 38 tasks spanning eight domains. We find that competence-related appraisal dimensions, particularly effort and ability, consistently match or outperform confidence across most settings. Effort additionally yields less overoptimistic estimates that remain stable across model sizes. In contrast, affective dimensions provide marginally predictive signals. Furthermore, the most informative dimension varies systematically with task characteristics: effort is most predictive for reasoning-intensive tasks, while ability and confidence dominate on retrieval-oriented tasks. Broadly, our findings indicate that structured multidimensional self-assessment is a promising approach to improving the reliability and safety of language model deployment across diverse real-world settings.

</details>


### [140] [Tool Calling is Linearly Readable and Steerable in Language Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.07990v2)
*Zekun Wu,Ze Wang,Seonglae Cho,Yufei Yang,Adriano Koshiyama,Sahan Bulathwela,Maria Perez-Ortiz*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文发现工具调用智能体内部存在编码工具选择的激活方向，通过干预该方向可以切换工具并预测错误，在多种模型上验证了效果，但在多轮场景下不稳定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前无法在工具调用错误发生前及时发现并阻止，可能导致严重后果，需要一种方法从模型内部检测错误。

Method: 在模型激活空间中识别每对工具对应的方向，通过添加该方向干预工具选择；并利用该方向的不确定性来预测错误。

Result: 在合成和真实API基准上，指令微调模型工具切换准确率达77-100%；基础模型内部表示已携带工具信息；不确定性标志错误率高21倍。

Conclusion: 通过内部方向可以可靠地控制和预测单轮工具选择，但多轮场景下效果不稳定，需要进一步研究。

中文摘要：当工具调用智能体选错了工具时，失败在工具执行之前是不可见的：邮件被发送了，会议被错过了。随着智能体承担越来越重要的行动，一次糟糕的工具调用可能会造成真正的损害。目前我们无法在内部审视模型并在错误发生之前捕捉它；本文表明我们可以做到。在模型内部，工具的选择由激活空间中的一个单一方向承载，每对工具对应一个方向。在生成过程中添加该方向会切换模型选择的工具。在涵盖Gemma 3、Qwen 3、Qwen 2.5和Llama 3.1（270M到27B）的12个指令微调模型和6个基础模型上，这在4B+指令微调模型上的15个工具合成基准测试中达到了83-100%的准确率，在真实API基准测试τ-bench airline上达到了77-94%的准确率。紧随其后的JSON参数会自动适应新工具的模式，因此只切换名称就足够了。相同的每工具方向也可以在错误发生之前标记出可能的错误：模型在两个工具之间不确定的查询失败率比不确定的查询高出21倍（Gemma 3 27B）。这不仅仅是主题注入：相同幅度的随机向量给出了0%的切换率，而单个领域内（共享一个主题的14个航空工具）的探针仍然可以以61-89%的top-1准确率读取模型将调用哪个工具（覆盖五个4B-14B模型）。即使是基础模型在能够输出正确工具之前内部已经携带了正确的工具：通过读取模型内部状态（余弦读出）在BFCL上恢复了61-82%的准确率，而基础模型生成仅有2-10%，这表明预训练形成了表示，而指令微调后来将其连接到输出。我们的结果涵盖了单轮、固定菜单设置；在多轮智能体循环中，相同的干预不太稳定（匹配基线增益或损失高达30个百分点，没有一致的方向）。

Original abstract: When a tool-calling agent picks the wrong tool, the failure is invisible until execution: the email gets sent, the meeting gets missed. As agents take on consequential actions, one bad tool call can do real damage. We currently have no way to look inside the model and catch the mistake before it happens; this paper shows that we can. Inside the model, the choice of tool is carried by a single direction in activation space, one direction per pair of tools. Adding that direction during generation switches which tool the model picks. Across 12 instruction-tuned and 6 base models spanning Gemma 3, Qwen 3, Qwen 2.5, and Llama 3.1 (270M to 27B), this works at 83-100% accuracy on 4B+ instruction-tuned models on a 15-tool synthetic benchmark and at 77-94% on the real-API benchmark $τ$-bench airline. The JSON arguments that follow automatically adapt to the new tool's schema, so flipping the name is enough. The same per-tool directions also flag likely errors before they happen: queries where the model is unsure between two tools fail 21x more often than queries where it is not (Gemma 3 27B). This is not just topic injection: random vectors at the same magnitude give a 0% switch rate, and a probe within a single domain (14 airline tools that share one topic) still reads which tool the model will call at top-1 61-89% across five 4B-14B models. Even base models already carry the right tool internally before they can emit it: reading the chosen tool off the model's internal state (cosine readout) recovers 61-82% accuracy on BFCL while base generation lands at 2-10%, suggesting pretraining forms the representation and instruction tuning later wires it to the output. Our results cover single-turn, fixed-menu settings; on multi-turn agent loops the same intervention is less stable (matched-baseline gain or loss of up to 30 percentage points with no consistent direction).

</details>


### [141] [CA-SQL: Complexity-Aware Inference Time Reasoning for Text-to-SQL via Exploration and Compute Budget Allocation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08057v1)
*James Petullo,Nianwen Xue*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: Text-to-SQL任务中基于复杂度分配计算预算的推理方法，属于coding agent探索策略。

TL;DR: CA-SQL通过动态探索广度、进化搜索提示播种和投票方法，在BIRD基准挑战任务上达到SOTA 51.72%，仅用GPT-4o-mini。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在BIRD基准的困难任务上表现不佳，主要原因是解空间探索不足，无法发现可进一步优化的候选查询。

Method: 提出CA-SQL流水线，利用任务估计难度动态调整候选解探索广度；基于进化搜索原理的自定义提示播种方法激发探索；使用新颖投票方法选择最佳候选解。

Result: 在BIRD开发集挑战任务上达到51.72%准确率，整体执行准确率61.06%，Soft F1 68.77%，超越其他上下文学习方法。

Conclusion: CA-SQL通过动态探索和进化搜索有效提升Text-to-SQL在困难任务上的性能，证明了小模型也能达到竞争力结果。

中文摘要：尽管最近在推理时学习方面的进展提高了LLM在Text-to-SQL任务上的推理能力，但当前的解决方案在处理Bird-Bench（BIRD）基准中最具挑战性的任务时仍然表现不佳。这是由于解空间探索不足，而解空间探索是发现有希望的候选查询的必要条件，这些查询可以进一步优化以产生正确的输出。为了解决这一挑战，我们引入了CA-SQL，一种新颖的Text-to-SQL流水线，它利用任务的估计难度动态调整生成候选解时的探索广度。此外，我们使用了一种基于进化搜索原理的自定义提示播种方法，以进一步激发基础LLM的探索行为，并采用一种新颖的投票方法在搜索结束时选择最佳候选解。实验表明，仅使用GPT-4o-mini，我们的方法在BIRD开发集问题的“挑战”级别上达到了51.72%的最新准确率，优于其他上下文学习方法，甚至包括那些使用更大模型的方法。总体而言，我们的方法在BIRD开发数据集上达到了61.06%的执行准确率和68.77%的Soft F1分数，具有竞争力。

Original abstract: While recent advancements in inference-time learning have improved LLM reasoning on Text-to-SQL tasks, current solutions still struggle to perform well on the most challenging tasks in the Bird-Bench (BIRD) benchmark. This is due to inadequate solution space exploration, which is necessary to uncover promising candidate queries that can be further refined to produce the correct output. To address this challenge, we introduce CA-SQL, a novel Text-to-SQL pipeline that utilizes the estimated difficulty of a task to dynamically scale the breadth of the exploration for generating solution candidates. In addition, we use a custom prompt seeding method, based on principles of evolutionary search, to further elicit exploratory behavior from the base LLM and a novel voting method to select the best candidate solution at the end of the search. Experiments demonstrate that our solution achieves a state-of-the-art score of 51.72% on the "challenging" tier of BIRD development set problems, using only GPT-4o-mini, out-performing other in-context learning approaches, even those that leverage larger models. Overall, our method attains a competitive 61.06% execution accuracy and 68.77% Soft F1 score on the BIRD development dataset.

### [142] [The Memory Curse: How Expanded Recall Erodes Cooperative Intent in LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08060v1)
*Jiayuan Liu,Tianqin Li,Shiyi Du,Xin Luo,Haoxuan Zeng,Emanuel Tewolde,Tai Sing Lee,Tonghan Wang,Carl Kingsford,Vincent Conitzer*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 研究多agent中记忆长度对合作的影响，对agent设计有启发。

TL;DR: 扩大LLM上下文窗口在多智能体社会困境中降低合作，原因在于前瞻意图侵蚀，而非内存长度；去除思维链可缓解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究上下文窗口扩展对多智能体合作的影响及其失败机制。

Method: 通过7个LLM在4个社会困境游戏中实验，分析推理轨迹、微调、内存净化和消融思维链。

Result: 在18/28设置中合作退化，前瞻意图侵蚀是主因，思维链放大问题。

Conclusion: 记忆是主动决定因素，需根据推理模式管理记忆内容。

中文摘要：上下文窗口扩展通常被视为LLM的一种直接能力提升，但我们发现它在多智能体社会困境中系统性地失败。在500轮次的7个LLM和4个游戏中，扩大可访问的历史记录在28个模型-游戏设置中的18个中降低了合作，我们将这种模式称为记忆诅咒。我们通过三个分析隔离了潜在机制。首先，对378,000个推理轨迹的词汇分析将这种崩溃与前瞻意图的侵蚀而非偏执加剧联系起来。我们通过目标微调作为认知探针验证了这一点：一个仅在前瞻轨迹上训练的LoRA适配器缓解了退化，并零样本迁移到不同游戏。其次，内存净化将提示长度固定，同时用合成的合作记录替换可见历史，这大幅恢复了合作，证明触发因素是内存内容而非长度本身。最后，消除显式思维链推理通常减少了崩溃，表明深思熟虑矛盾地放大了记忆诅咒。这些结果共同将记忆重塑为多智能体行为的主动决定因素：更长的回忆可以根据其引发的推理模式破坏或支持合作。

Original abstract: Context window expansion is often treated as a straightforward capability upgrade for LLMs, but we find it systematically fails in multi-agent social dilemmas. Across 7 LLMs and 4 games over 500 rounds, expanding accessible history degrades cooperation in 18 of 28 model--game settings, a pattern we term the memory curse. We isolate the underlying mechanism through three analyses. First, lexical analysis of 378,000 reasoning traces associates this breakdown with eroding forward-looking intent rather than rising paranoia. We validate this using targeted fine-tuning as a cognitive probe: a LoRA adapter trained exclusively on forward-looking traces mitigates the decay and transfers zero-shot to distinct games. Second, memory sanitization holds prompt length fixed while replacing visible history with synthetic cooperative records, which restores cooperation substantially, proving the trigger is memory content, not length alone. Finally, ablating explicit Chain-of-Thought reasoning often reduces the collapse, showing that deliberation paradoxically amplifies the memory curse. Together, these results recast memory as an active determinant of multi-agent behavior: longer recall can either destabilize or support cooperation depending on the reasoning patterns it elicits.

### [143] [AIPO: Learning to Reason from Active Interaction](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08401v2)
*Junnan Liu,Linhao Luo,Thuy-Trang Vu,Gholamreza Haffari*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 利用多智能体协作（验证、知识、推理智能体）增强LLM推理训练，其交互探索机制可迁移至代码优化智能体。

TL;DR: AIPO通过主动多智能体交互扩展LLM推理能力边界，提升强化学习效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RL算法受限于策略模型自身能力边界，而专家演示方法样本效率低且限制探索空间。

Method: 提出AIPO框架，引入验证、知识和推理三个协作智能体，在训练中提供细粒度指导，并使用重要性采样和裁剪策略缓解离策略偏差和梯度消失。

Result: 在AIME、MATH500、GPQA-Diamond和LiveCodeBench等基准上，AIPO持续提升推理性能，并泛化到不同模型和算法。

Conclusion: AIPO有效扩展了策略模型的推理能力边界，且训练后可独立推理。

中文摘要：近年来，大型语言模型（LLMs）的进展展示了显著的推理能力，这主要由可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）所推动。然而，现有的强化学习算法面临一个根本性限制：它们的探索在很大程度上仍受限于策略模型自身的能力边界。尽管近期的方法引入外部专家演示来扩展这一边界，但它们通常依赖于完整的轨迹级指导，这导致样本效率低、信息稀疏，并可能将探索限制在静态的指导空间中。受多智能体系统潜力的启发，我们提出了AIPO，这是一个增强的强化学习框架，通过在探索过程中进行主动的多智能体交互来提升LLM的推理能力。具体来说，AIPO使策略模型能够在遇到推理瓶颈时主动咨询三个功能协作智能体：验证智能体、知识智能体和推理智能体，从而在训练过程中获得细粒度且有针对性的指导，以主动扩展其能力边界。我们进一步引入了一个定制的重要性采样系数以及一个裁剪策略，以缓解从智能体提供的反馈中学习时出现的离策略偏差和梯度消失问题。训练完成后，策略模型能够独立进行推理，无需依赖协作智能体。在包括AIME、MATH500、GPQA-Diamond和LiveCodeBench在内的多种推理基准上的广泛实验表明，AIPO持续提升了推理性能，在不同策略模型和RLVR算法上具有稳健的泛化能力，并有效扩展了策略模型的推理能力边界。

Original abstract: Recent advances in large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated remarkable reasoning capabilities, largely stimulated by Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR). However, existing RL algorithms face a fundamental limitation: their exploration remains largely constrained by the inherent capability boundary of the policy model. Although recent methods introduce external expert demonstrations to extend this boundary, they typically rely on complete trajectory-level guidance, which is sample-inefficient, information-sparse, and may confine exploration to a static guidance space. Inspired by the potential of multi-agent systems, we propose $\textbf{AIPO}$, an enhanced reinforcement learning framework that improves LLM reasoning through active multi-agent interaction during exploration. Specifically, AIPO enables the policy model to proactively consult three functional collaborative agents, $\textit{Verify Agent}$, $\textit{Knowledge Agent}$, and $\textit{Reasoning Agent}$, when encountering reasoning bottlenecks, thereby receiving fine-grained and targeted guidance to actively expand its capability boundary during training. We further introduce a tailored importance sampling coefficient together with a clipping strategy to mitigate the off-policy bias and gradient vanishing issues that arise when learning from agent-provided feedback. After training, the policy model performs reasoning independently without relying on collaborative agents. Extensive experiments on diverse reasoning benchmarks, including AIME, MATH500, GPQA-Diamond, and LiveCodeBench, show that AIPO consistently improves reasoning performance, generalizes robustly across different policy models and RLVR algorithms, and effectively expands the reasoning capability boundary of the policy model.

</details>


### [144] [A Semantic-Sampling Framework for Evaluating Calibration in Open-Ended Question Answering](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08432v1)
*Zhanliang Wang,Jiancong Xiao,Ruochen Jin,Shu Yang,Bojian Hou,Li Shen*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 提出语义采样校准评估框架，可应用于智能体的置信度校准与可靠性评测。

TL;DR: 提出Sem-ECE框架，通过语义聚类采样答案的置信度来评估开放式问答中LLM的校准，包括两个渐近无偏的估计量，实验证明其优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有校准评估方法在开放式问答中存在局限，如logit方法受限、口头报告过于自信、采样方法无明确目标，亟需更合适的评估框架。

Method: 从LLM采样多个答案，语义聚类后以类别频率作为置信度，构建两个估计量：Sem1-ECE（同样本自洽性）和Sem2-ECE（留出法分离答案选择与置信评估），并证明渐近无偏性。

Result: 在三个开放式QA基准和五个商业LLM上，Sem-ECE优于口头置信度和现有采样方法，与理论预测一致，且Sem1与Sem2的差距可诊断问题难度。

Conclusion: Sem-ECE是有效的开放式QA校准评估框架，弥补了现有方法的不足，在无logit时提供可靠替代方案。

中文摘要：校准衡量模型预测的置信度与其经验准确率是否一致，对于在高风险领域（如医学和法律）可靠部署大型语言模型（LLM）至关重要。虽然近期大量工作聚焦于改进LLM的校准，但在现实场景中如何评估校准这一同样重要的问题仍不成熟。开放式问答（QA）是现代LLM最常见的部署场景，现有评估方法在此存在不足：基于logit的指标需要受限的输出格式和内部概率；口头报告的置信度是自我报告的且往往过度自信；基于采样的方法依赖特定任务的提取规则，且缺乏明确的有限样本目标。我们提出Sem-ECE（语义采样期望校准误差），一个针对开放式QA的校准评估框架，该框架从模型中采样答案，将其分组为语义类别，并使用所得频率作为置信度。我们研究该框架内的两个估计量：Sem$_1$-ECE，即同一样本的自洽性分数；以及Sem$_2$-ECE，一种将答案选择与置信度评估分离的留出变体。我们证明两者都是渐近无偏的，并进一步表明它们在简单问题上一致，但在困难问题上出现分歧，且Sem$_2$实现严格更小的校准误差，因此它们的差距也可作为问题难度的诊断指标。在五个领先的商业LLM上针对三个开放式QA基准的实验与我们的理论预测一致，表明Sem-ECE优于口头报告置信度和现有基于采样的方法，同时在内部概率不可用时补充基于logit的评估。

Original abstract: Calibration measures whether a model's predicted confidence aligns with its empirical accuracy, and is central to the reliable deployment of large language models (LLMs) in high-stakes domains such as medicine and law. While much recent work focuses on improving LLM calibration, the equally important question of how to evaluate it in realistic settings remains underdeveloped. Open-ended question answering (QA), the most common deployment setting for modern LLMs, is where existing evaluation methods fall short: logit-based metrics need restricted output formats and internal probabilities; verbalized confidence is self-reported and often overconfident; and sampling-based methods rely on task-specific extraction rules without a clear finite-sample target. We introduce Sem-ECE (Semantic-Sampling Expected Calibration Error), a calibration evaluation framework for open-ended QA that samples answers from the model, groups them into semantic classes, and uses the resulting frequencies as confidence. We study two estimators within this framework: Sem$_1$-ECE, the same-sample self-consistency score, and Sem$_2$-ECE, a held-out variant that separates answer selection from confidence evaluation. We prove both are asymptotically unbiased, and further show that they agree on easy questions but diverge on hard ones with Sem$_2$ achieving strictly smaller calibration error, so their gap also serves as a diagnostic for question difficulty. Experiments on three open-ended QA benchmarks across five leading commercial LLMs match our theoretical predictions and show that Sem-ECE outperforms verbalized confidence and existing sampling-based methods, while complementing logit-based evaluation when internal probabilities are unavailable.

</details>


### [145] [PYTHALAB-MERA: Validation-Grounded Memory, Retrieval, and Acceptance Control for Frozen-LLM Coding Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2605.08468v1)
*Mehmet Iscan*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 针对编码agent的记忆、检索、验证控制器，直接相关coding agent。

TL;DR: 提出PYTHALAB-MERA，一个外部控制器，结合记忆和检索提升本地LLM在强化学习编码任务中的验证成功率，在严格验证下显著优于基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法（静态检索、长上下文提示、自我改进、执行反馈修复、强化学习）未联合提供验证基础的片段记忆、自适应检索-动作选择、延迟信用分配和结构化技能重用。

Method: 使用冻结的语言模型生成完整源文件，外部控制器决定记忆记录和AST派生技能进入提示，通过快速失败管道验证候选者，将验证结果转换为有界形状的奖励，并通过TD(lambda)风格的资格迹传播延迟信用。

Result: 在三个任务、三个重复、三次尝试预算的硬RL设置中，PYTHALAB-MERA通过8/9严格验证，而自我改进基线和GRACE扩展均通过0/9。

Conclusion: 外部记忆和检索控制器提高了验证成功率，但未建立通用代码合成、最先进性能、正式程序正确性或正式安全性。

中文摘要：基于本地LLM的编码代理越来越多地在通过执行反馈、持久状态和有界修复来获得正确性的环境中工作，而不是通过一个流畅的答案。静态检索、长上下文提示、自我改进、执行反馈修复以及模型权重的强化学习各自解决了这一场景中的一部分，但它们并没有联合提供验证基础的片段记忆、自适应检索-动作选择、延迟信用分配以及围绕冻结本地模型的结构化技能重用。我们引入了PYTHALAB-MERA，一个用于本地验证条件代码生成的轻量级外部控制器。冻结的语言模型提出完整的源文件；控制器决定哪些记忆记录和AST派生技能应进入下一个提示，通过快速失败管道验证每个候选者，将验证结果转换为有界形状的奖励，并通过TD(lambda)风格的资格迹传播延迟信用。我们在强化学习编码任务上评估该实现作为本地CLI工件，具有严格的验证门。在三个任务、三个重复和三次尝试预算的测量硬RL设置中，PYTHALAB-MERA通过了8/9的严格验证；自我改进基线和研究的GRACE扩展各通过0/9。这些结果支持一个刻意有界的声明：在这个记录的场景中，外部内存和检索控制器提高了验证成功率。它们并未建立通用代码合成、最先进性能、正式程序正确性或正式安全性。

Original abstract: Local LLM-based coding agents increasingly work in settings where correctness is earned through execution feedback, persistent state, and bounded repair, not through a single fluent answer. Static retrieval, long-context prompting, self-refinement, execution-feedback repair, and reinforcement learning over model weights each address part of this setting, but they do not jointly provide validation-grounded episodic memory, adaptive retrieval-action selection, delayed credit assignment, and structural skill reuse around a frozen local model. We introduce PYTHALAB-MERA, a lightweight external controller for local validation-conditioned code generation. The frozen language model proposes complete source files; the controller decides which memory records and AST-derived skills should enter the next prompt, validates each candidate through a fail-fast pipeline, converts validation outcomes into bounded shaped rewards, and propagates delayed credit through TD(lambda)-style eligibility traces. We evaluate the implementation as a local CLI artifact on reinforcement-learning coding tasks with strict validation gates. In the measured hard RL setting with three tasks, three repetitions, and a three-attempt budget, PYTHALAB-MERA passed 8/9 strict validations; the self-refinement baseline and the investigated GRACE extension each passed 0/9. These results support a deliberately bounded claim: in this recorded setting, the external memory-and-retrieval controller improved validation success. They do not establish general-purpose code synthesis, state-of-the-art performance, formal program correctness, or formal safety.

</details>
